d_botde_add_revolt_progress = {
	resize_temp_array = { args = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = args^0 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { ROOT.revolt_progress_change = temp_progress }
	ROOT = { BOTDE_add_collapse = yes }
}

AUS_debug_effect = {
	set_variable = { AUS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.52 }
	set_variable = { CRO.subject_revolt_progress = 0.28 }		
	set_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress = 0.46 }			
	set_variable = { CZE.subject_revolt_progress = 0.39 }	
	set_variable = { GAL.subject_revolt_progress = 0.52 }
	set_variable = { ITA.subject_revolt_progress = 0.12 }
	clear_array = global.constituents_array
	AUS = { set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 2 } }
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = AUS }
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = HUN }
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = CRO }
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = CZE }
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = GAL }
}

AUS_open_gui_click_effect = {
	get_sorted_scored_countries = {
		scorer = BOTDE_constituents_in_GUI_score
		array = ROOT.austria_subject_array
	}
	get_sorted_scored_countries = {
		scorer = BOTDE_minorities_in_GUI_score
		array = ROOT.austria_minority_array
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_clickme_flag }
		clr_global_flag = AUS_clickme_flag
	}
	set_country_flag = subject_unrest_window_open
	
	# a little trolling
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = schizo_value_enabled
		}
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				set_country_flag = schizo_value_on
			}
			60 = {
			
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = schizo_value_on
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = schizo_value
				distribution = uniform
				min = -0.15
				max = 0.15
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.schizo_value_var
				value = schizo_value
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = AUS_collapsed
						}
					}
					set_variable = { schizophrenic = AUS }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							HUN = {
								is_in_faction_with = AUS
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { schizophrenic = HUN }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							CZE = {
								is_in_faction_with = AUS
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { schizophrenic = CZE }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							CRO = {
								is_in_faction_with = AUS
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { schizophrenic = CRO }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							GAL = {
								is_in_faction_with = AUS
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { schizophrenic = GAL }
				}
			}
			AUS_do_schizo_test = yes
			var:schizophrenic = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
					value = schizo_value
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

subjects_minority_view_sort_button_click_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_minority_array_not_sorted }
		clr_global_flag = AUS_minority_array_not_sorted
	}
	else = { set_global_flag = AUS_minority_array_not_sorted }
	clear_array = ROOT.austria_minority_array
	get_sorted_scored_countries = {
		scorer = BOTDE_minorities_in_GUI_score
		array = ROOT.austria_minority_array
	}
}

constituents_minority_view_sort_button_click_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_constituents_array_not_sorted }
		clr_global_flag = AUS_constituents_array_not_sorted
	}
	else = { set_global_flag = AUS_constituents_array_not_sorted }
	clear_array = ROOT.austria_subject_array
	get_sorted_scored_countries = {
		scorer = BOTDE_constituents_in_GUI_score
		array = ROOT.austria_subject_array
	}
}

AUS_warning_check = {
	clear_array = ROOT.austria_warning_subject_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = global.AUS_all_possible_array
		var:v = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = subject_revolt_progress
					AUS_is_constituent_or_minority = yes
					check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.749 }
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = { ROOT.austria_warning_subject_array = THIS }
						has_war_with = AUS
						has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { ROOT.austria_warning_subject_array = v }
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war = no
				fifth_balkan_war = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.extra_value_war_exhaust = 0 }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = stability }
	set_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_party_pop_thing = party_popularity@ruling_party }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable  = { revolt_rate_rising = -0.03 }
	divide_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_party_pop_thing = 100 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = revolt_rate_party_pop_thing }
	add_to_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = AUS.extra_value }
	add_to_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = global.extra_value_war_exhaust }
	add_to_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = global.extra_collapse_federalizing }
	add_to_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = modifier@BOTDE_revolt_rate_modifier }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = AUS_root_out_class_hatred
				has_completed_focus = AUS_to_these_united_states
				has_completed_focus = AUS_test_of_time
				has_completed_focus = AUS_charity_and_unity
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = 0.002 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { fifth_balkan_war = yes }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = 0.005 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_AUS_continuous_collapse_decrease_flag }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = 0.01 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { AUS.revolt_progress_change = revolt_rate_rising }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change < 1 } } #for modifier tooltips
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise: [?AUS.revolt_progress_change]"
		BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
	}
}

CONST_do_additional_revolt_progress = {
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = num_of_factories }
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_ROOT = num_battalions }
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_AUS = AUS.num_battalions }
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability = AUS.stability }
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_THIS_stability = stability }
	set_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_AUS = AUS.num_of_factories }
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_THIS_stability = 3 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability = CONST_revolt_rate_rising_THIS_stability }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability = -1.2 }
	
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = 120 }
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_ROOT = 10000 }
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_AUS = 50000 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability = -3.5 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_ROOT }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability }
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = 20 }
	divide_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising_AUS = 7500 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_AUS }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = CONST_revolt_rate_rising_AUS }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = THIS.extra_value }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = global.extra_value_war_exhaust }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = global.extra_collapse_federalizing }
	add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = modifier@BOTDE_revolt_rate_modifier }
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }
		add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = -0.015 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { fifth_balkan_war = yes }
		add_to_temp_variable = { CONST_revolt_rate_rising = -0.005 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_AUS_continuous_collapse_decrease_flag }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolt_rate_rising = 0.01 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { THIS.revolt_progress_change = CONST_revolt_rate_rising }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change < 1 } } #for modifier tooltips
		log = "[GetDateText]: [THIS.GetName]: CONST_do_additional_revolt_progress: [?revolt_progress_change] CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability: [?CONST_revolt_rate_rising_stability] CONST_revolt_rate_rising_THIS_stability: [?CONST_revolt_rate_rising_THIS_stability] CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_ROOT: [?CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_ROOT] CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_AUS: [?CONST_revolt_rate_rising_battalion_AUS]"
		BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
	}
}

AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise_counterintel = {
	set_temp_variable = { AUS_intel_subtract = modifier@intelligence_agency_defense }
	divide_temp_variable = { AUS_intel_subtract = 750 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { ROOT.revolt_progress_change = AUS_intel_subtract }
	BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
}

AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise_operative_mission = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AUS = {
				any_operative_leader = { operative_leader_mission = counter_intelligence }
			}
			NOT = {
				is_preparing_operation = { target = any_country }
				is_running_operation  = { target = any_country }
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { ROOT.revolt_progress_change = -0.003 }
		BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
	}
}

AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise_operative_mission_diplo_pressure = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AUS = {
				any_operative_leader = { operative_leader_mission = diplomatic_pressure }
				NOT = {
					is_preparing_operation = { target = any_country }
					is_running_operation  = { target = any_country }
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { ROOT.revolt_progress_change = -0.003 }
		BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
	}
}

AUS_black_monday_effect = {
	if = { 
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = AUS_collapsed } } #for testing austrian collapse at game start
		if = {
			limit = { has_political_power > 0 }
			set_political_power = 0
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		add_ideas = AUS_bm_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { AUS_BM_value = 1 }
			complete_national_focus = AUS_berlin_stock_market_crash
			country_event = {
				id = italianrepublic.150
				days = 5
				random_hours = 72
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.39
				days = 4
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.13
				days = 20
				random_hours = 300
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausflavor.169
				days = 2
				random_hours = 72
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_elect_CS_1940 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_ender_1940
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = AUS_Otto_Ender_hog_sco
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_miklas_1940
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = AUS_Wilhelm_Miklas_hog_sco
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_buresch_1940
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = AUS_Karl_Buresch_hog_ade
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_macek_1940
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_no_more_illyrian_revolt
		set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_CRO_revolt
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CRO_Vladko_Macek_hog_sli
		set_country_leader_ideology = soccon_agrarianism_subtype
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_soccon_agrarianism_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_bethlen_1940
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_disable_hungarian_revolt
		set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_HUN_revolt
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = HUN_Istvan_Bethlen_hog_ade
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	else = {
		set_country_flag = AUS_ender_1940
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = AUS_Otto_Ender_hog_sco
		custom_effect_tooltip = soccon_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		news_event = {
			id = bdeausnews.28
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_figl_1940
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_christian_democracy_subtype
		custom_effect_tooltip = pataut_pataut_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_raab_1940
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_christian_democracy_subtype
		custom_effect_tooltip = pataut_pataut_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = AUS_Julius_Raab_hog_sco
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_tildy_1940
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_christian_democracy_subtype
		custom_effect_tooltip = pataut_pataut_christian_democracy_subtype_swap_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_disable_hungarian_revolt
		set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_HUN_revolt
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = HUN_Zoltan_Tildy_hog_sco
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_tarnowski_1940

AUS_raise_austro_german_tensions = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = AUS_tro_german_tensions_rise
		add_to_variable = { global.AUS_GER_tensions = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.AUS_GER_tensions > 2 } }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = AUS
						tag = GER
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.52
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_lower_austro_german_tensions = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = AUS_tro_german_tensions_lower
		add_to_variable = { global.AUS_GER_tensions = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_GER_tensions_lvl_1
				check_variable = { global.AUS_GER_tensions < 3 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = AUS
						tag = GER
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.53
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#### Add constituent revolt ####

#requires temp variable revolt_progress_change
#is scoped to country i.e 
# HUN = { 
#	set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.01 }
#	BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
#}

BOTDE_add_collapse = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AUS_is_constituent_or_minority = yes
			AUS_can_collapse = yes
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = BOTDE_collapse_tt
			add_to_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = revolt_progress_change }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
					min = 0
					max = 0.75
				}
			}
			else = {
				clamp_variable = {
					var = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: BOTDE_add_collapse: revolt_progress_change: [?revolt_progress_change] THIS.subject_revolt_progress: [?THIS.subject_revolt_progress]"
			BOTDE_check_for_constituent_revolt = yes
			AUS_warning_check = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUS = { has_country_flag = subject_unrest_window_open }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = AUS_minority_array_not_sorted }
				}
				clear_array = AUS.austria_minority_array
				get_sorted_scored_countries = {
					scorer = BOTDE_minorities_in_GUI_score
					array = AUS.austria_minority_array
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_check_for_constituent_revolt = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 1 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 1 }
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_global_flag = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war
				has_global_flag = AUS_pause_collapse_flag
				OR = {
					AUS = { is_ai = yes }
					date < 1937.01.01
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = HUN }
			country_event = revolt.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = CRO }
			country_event = revolt.2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = CZE }
			country_event = revolt.3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GAL }
			country_event = revolt.4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.8 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.8 }
			}
			has_global_flag = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war
			AUS_is_constituent_or_minority = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HUN
				NOT = {
					AUS = {
						has_active_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_HUN_leave_deadline
						has_active_mission = BOTDE_hungarian_revolt_headsup
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = { activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_HUN_leave_deadline }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CRO
				NOT = {
					AUS = {
						has_active_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_CRO_leave_deadline
						has_active_mission = BOTDE_illyrian_revolt_headsup
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = { activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_CRO_leave_deadline }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CZE
				NOT = {
					AUS = {
						has_active_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_CZE_leave_deadline
						has_active_mission = BOTDE_czech_revolt_headsup
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = { activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_CZE_leave_deadline }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GAL
				NOT = {
					AUS = {
						has_active_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_GAL_leave_deadline
						has_active_mission = BOTDE_galician_revolt_headsup
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = wants_to_revolt
			AUS = { activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_GAL_leave_deadline }
		}
	}
	set_variable = { global.AUS_tags_over_94_revolt = 0 }
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.AUS_all_possible_array
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = AUS
					has_event_target = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.95 }
						check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.95 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { global.AUS_tags_over_94_revolt = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable { global.AUS_tags_over_94_revolt > 0 }
			NOT = { 
				has_global_flag = no_more_collapse
				has_global_flag = AUS_collapsed
				has_global_flag = AUS_pause_collapse_flag
				has_country_flag = do_not_show_kx_alerts
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:kx_alert_aus_const_revolt_incoming }
			set_temp_variable = { alert_color = 2 }
			add_kx_alert_unless_exists = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable { global.AUS_tags_over_94_revolt < 1 }
				has_global_flag = no_more_collapse
				has_global_flag = AUS_collapsed
				has_global_flag = AUS_pause_collapse_flag
				has_country_flag = do_not_show_kx_alerts
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:kx_alert_aus_const_revolt_incoming }
			remove_kx_alert = yes
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_add_revolt_rate = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AUS_is_constituent_or_minority = yes
			AUS_can_collapse = yes
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = BOTDE_revolt_rate_tt
			add_to_variable = { THIS.extra_value = revolt_rate_change }
		}
	}
}

AUS_raise_govt_percentage_1 = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = govt_raise_1
	add_to_variable = { global.government_percentage = 0.01 }
	clamp_variable = { var = global.government_percentage min = 0 max = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { constituent_federalizing_temp = global.government_percentage }
	divide_temp_variable = { constituent_federalizing_temp = 2 }
	
	set_variable = { global.constituent_federalizing = constituent_federalizing_temp }	
	divide_temp_variable = { constituent_federalizing_temp = 30 }
	
	set_variable = { global.extra_collapse_federalizing = constituent_federalizing_temp }
}

AUS_do_cultural_festivity_thing = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				state = 1123
			}
		}
		SVK = {
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = -0.15 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				state = 1140
			}
		}
		WSU = {

AUS_raise_vienna_tenseness = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BOTDE_vienna_tenseness_raised
	add_to_variable = { AUS.paramiliary_tenseness = 1 }
}

AUS_change_paramilitary_schutzbund = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BOTDE_schutzbund_takes_here
	hidden_effect = {
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = AUS_schutzbund_presence
		}
		add_to_variable = { AUS.schutzbund_presence = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = AUS_frontfighters_presence
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { AUS.frontfighters_presence = 1 }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_frontfighters_presence } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = AUS_ostmarkische_sturmscharen_presence
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { AUS.sturmscharen_presence = 1 }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_ostmarkische_sturmscharen_presence } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = AUS_heimwehr_presence
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { AUS.heimwehr_presence = 1 }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_heimwehr_presence } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = AUS_ordo_novi_templi_presence
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { AUS.ordo_novi_templi_presence = 1 }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_ordo_novi_templi_presence }
		}
	}
}

AUS_paramilitary_result = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_belligerent_1_victory_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_heimwehr_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_ont = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_heimwehr = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_schutzbund_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_schutzbund_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_schutzbund_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_schutzbund_v_ont = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_schutzbund = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_frontfighters_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_ont = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_frontfighters = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_ont = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_sturmscharen = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_ont_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_ont_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_ont_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_ont_v_schutzbund = yes 
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_ont = yes
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_belligerent_2_victory_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_schutzbund_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_heimwehr = yes
					AUS_ont_v_heimwehr = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_heimwehr = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_heimwehr_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_schutzbund = yes
					AUS_ont_v_schutzbund = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_schutzbund = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_schutzbund_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_frontfighters = yes
					AUS_ont_v_frontfighters = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_frontfighters = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_schutzbund_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_sturmscharen = yes
					AUS_ont_v_sturmscharen = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_sturmscharen = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AUS_schutzbund_v_ont = yes
					AUS_frontfighters_v_ont = yes
					AUS_sturmscharen_v_ont = yes
					AUS_heimwehr_v_ont = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = BOTDE_paramilitary_target_state
				}
				AUS_change_paramilitary_ont = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

THIS_add_minority_paramilitary = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = SLO }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_slovene = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = WSU }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_ukrainian = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = BOS }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_bosniak = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = PGU }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_deutschbohmen = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = CPU }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_ruthenian = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = TRS }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_transylvanian = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = SVK }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_slovak = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = SKS }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_serbian = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = BUK }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_bukovinian = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { is_core_of = BAN }
		AUS_change_minority_paramilitary_banatian = yes
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { infrastructure > 0 }
			set_temp_variable_to_random = temp_damage
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = temp_damage
				min = 0.2
				max = 0.8
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = temp_damage
			}
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_stability = -0.05 }
		}
	}
}

AUS_remove_minority_paramilitary = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_slovene_home_guard_presence } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_slovene_home_guard_presence }

		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GAL_UVO_presence }
		subtract_from_variable = { WSU.paramilitary_value = 1 }
	}
	if = {

		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CRO_chetnik_presence }

	}
	if = {

		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CRO_green_cadres_presence }
		subtract_from_variable = { BOS.paramilitary_value = 1 }
	}
	if = {

		subtract_from_variable = { SVK.paramilitary_value = 1 }

minority_paramilitary_gain_unrest = {
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = SVK } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SVK = {
					is_ally_with = FROM.owner
					is_ally_with = AUS
				}
			}
			FROM.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.1 }
				BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS_raise_slovaks = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = TRS } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRS = {
					is_ally_with = FROM.owner
					is_ally_with = AUS
				}
			}
			FROM.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.1 }
				BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS_raise_transylvanians = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = SLO } }
		AUS_raise_slovenes = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = BOS } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				BOS = {
					is_ally_with = FROM.owner
					is_ally_with = AUS
				}
			}
			FROM.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.1 }
				BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS_raise_bosnians = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = PGU } }
		hidden_effect = { AUS_raise_deutschbohmen = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = PGU_on_array }
			effect_tooltip = { AUS_raise_deutschbohmen = yes }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = CPU } }
		AUS_raise_ruthenians = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = WSU } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				WSU = {
					is_ally_with = FROM.owner
					is_ally_with = AUS
				}
			}
			FROM.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.1 }
				BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS_raise_ukrainians = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = SKS } }
		AUS_raise_serbians = yes
	}
}

AUS_add_to_DWV = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = THIS_JOINS_DWV
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { AUS.DWV_members = THIS.id } } }
			add_to_array = { AUS.DWV_members = THIS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = DWV_alt_enabled }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 5 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_5_alt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 4 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_4_alt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 3 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_3_alt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 2 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_2_alt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 1 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_1_alt
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_0_alt
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 5 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 4 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 3 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 2 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AUS.DWV_upgrade = 1 } }
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_1
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = AUS_DWV_0
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_remove_from_DWV = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = THIS_LEAVES_DWV
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { AUS.DWV_members = THIS.id } }
			remove_from_array = { AUS.DWV_members = THIS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			AUS_DWV_0
			AUS_DWV_1
			AUS_DWV_2
			AUS_DWV_3
			AUS_DWV_4
			AUS_DWV_5
			AUS_DWV_0_alt
			AUS_DWV_1_alt
			AUS_DWV_2_alt
			AUS_DWV_3_alt
			AUS_DWV_4_alt
			AUS_DWV_5_alt
		}
	}
}

AUS_swap_DWV_to_alt = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = swap_DWV_to_alt_tt
		set_global_flag = DWV_alt_enabled
		every_country = {
			limit = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_0 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_0
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_0_alt
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_1
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_1_alt
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_2
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_2_alt
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_3
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_3_alt
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_4 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_4
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_4_alt
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_DWV_5 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_DWV_5
					add_idea = AUS_DWV_5_alt
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_check_DWV_swap_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = AUS
			AUS_DWV_member = yes
		}
		AUS_swap_DWV_to_alt = yes
	}
}

EUU_unite_europe_effect = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = EUU_unite_europe_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = EUU
					EUU_EU_member = yes
					any_allied_country = {
						AND = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							EUU_EU_member = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_temp_array = { temp_faction_members = THIS.id }
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				EUU_EU_member = yes
				NOT = { tag = EUU }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
				add_core_of = EUU
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { EUU_EU_member = no }
				get_current_government_type = yes
				EUU = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomous_state = kr_nominal_puppet
					}
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = EUU }
			every_scientist = { set_nationality = EUU }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS } }
				remove_from_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS }
			}
			EUU = {
				transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
				transfer_int_upgrade = yes
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		EUU = {
			set_global_flag = EUU_federalized
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_PANEURO
			news_event = bdeeunews.1
			country_event = {
				id = super.27
				hours = 2
			}
			create_faction_from_template = {
				template = faction_template_paneuropa
				name = faction_paneuropa
				icon = GFX_faction_paneuropa
				color = { 0.25 0.22 0.5 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { temp_faction_members = THIS.id }
					exists = yes
				}
				EUU = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.EU_economic_integration_flat = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.EU_army_xp_pool = 0 }
	}
}

EUU_add_to_EU = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = THIS_JOINS_EU
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS } } }
			add_to_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = EUU_allocations} } }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = EUU_allocations }
		}
	}
}

EUU_remove_from_EU = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { EUU.EUU_EU_members = THIS }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = EUU_allocations} }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = EUU_allocations }
	}
	clear_variable = THIS.extra_pp_allocation
	clear_variable = THIS.EUU_civ_allocation_penalty
}

EUU_find_half_calculation = {
	set_variable = { global.european_countries = 0 }
	every_country = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = RUS
					tag = TUR
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { global.european_countries = 1 }
		}
	}
	#Find half of that number
	set_temp_variable = { half_life = global.european_countries }
	divide_temp_variable = { half_life = 2 }
	round_temp_variable = half_life
	set_variable = { global.half_of_euro_countries = half_life }
}

EUU_find_third_calculation = {
	set_variable = { global.european_countries = 0 }
	every_country = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = RUS
					tag = TUR
					tag = NSW
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { global.european_countries = 1 }
		}
	}
	#Find half of that number
	set_temp_variable = { half_life_3 = global.european_countries }
	divide_temp_variable = { half_life_3 = 3 }
	round_temp_variable = half_life_3
	set_variable = { global.third_of_euro_countries = half_life_3 }
}

EUU_get_pressure_gain = {
	set_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain_monthly = 0 }
	every_country = {
		limit = { EUU_EU_member = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { local_pressure = political_power_daily }
		set_temp_variable = { extra_pp_allocation = THIS.extra_pp_allocation }
		multiply_temp_variable = { extra_pp_allocation = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain = local_pressure }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain = extra_pp_allocation }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { weekly = global.EU_pressure_gain }
	multiply_temp_variable = { weekly = 7 }
	add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain_weekly = 7 }
	set_temp_variable = { monthly = global.EU_pressure_gain }
	multiply_temp_variable = { monthly = 30 }
	add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_gain_monthly = monthly }
}

EUU_calculate_army_factories = {
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_divisions_var = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_battalions_var = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_factories_var = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_dockyards = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_mils = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_total_civs = 0 }
	every_country = {
		limit = { EUU_EU_member = yes }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_divisions_var = num_divisions }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_battalions_var = num_battalions }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_factories_var = num_of_factories }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_dockyards = num_of_naval_factories }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_mils = num_of_military_factories }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_total_civs = num_of_civilian_factories }
	}
}

EUU_add_pressure_from_gain = {
	add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_value = global.EU_pressure_gain }
}

EUU_add_pressure_from_gain_week = {
	set_temp_variable = { weekly = global.EU_pressure_gain }
	multiply_temp_variable = { weekly = 7 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = EUU_federalized }
		multiply_temp_variable = { weekly = 5 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { global.EU_pressure_value = weekly }
}

EUU_calculate_necessary_pressure = {
	set_temp_variable = { pressure_factories = num_of_factories	}
	set_temp_variable = { pressure_population = max_manpower_k }
	set_temp_variable = { pressure_army = num_battalions }
	set_temp_variable = { pressure_total = 0 }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { pressure_factories = 10 }
	divide_temp_variable = { pressure_population = 15 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { pressure_army = 4 }
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { pressure_total = pressure_factories }
	add_to_temp_variable = { pressure_total = pressure_population }
	add_to_temp_variable = { pressure_total = pressure_army }

	round_temp_variable = pressure_total

	set_temp_variable = { temp_modulo = pressure_total }
	modulo_temp_variable = { temp_modulo = 50 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { pressure_total = temp_modulo }

	log = "[GetDateText]: [THIS.GetName]: EUU_calculate_necessary_pressure: pressure_total = [?pressure_total] temp_modulo = [?temp_modulo]"
	
	capital_scope = {
		owner = { set_variable = { necessary_EU_pressure = pressure_total } }
	}
}

EU_add_one_civ_to_total = {
	add_to_variable = { global.EUU_civ_allocation_total = 1 }
}

EU_remove_one_civ_to_total = {
	subtract_from_variable = { global.EUU_civ_allocation_total = 1 }
}

EU_faction_do_economic_integration = {
	set_temp_variable = { total_integration_civs_count = global.EUU_civ_allocation_total }
	set_temp_variable = { necessary_integration = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	set_temp_variable = { necessary_integration_total_factories = global.EU_total_factories_var }
	multiply_temp_variable = { necessary_integration = 200 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { necessary_integration_total_factories = 2 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { necessary_integration = necessary_integration_total_factories }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { total_integration_civs_count = 1.5 }
	add_to_variable = { global.EU_economic_integration_flat = total_integration_civs_count }

	set_temp_variable = { economic_percent_temp = global.EU_economic_integration_flat }
	multiply_temp_variable = { economic_percent_temp = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { economic_percent_temp = necessary_integration }
	divide_temp_variable = { economic_percent_temp = 10 }
	
	#Find percentage
	set_variable = { global.EU_economic_integration_percentage = economic_percent_temp }
}

EU_faction_do_military_integration = {
	set_temp_variable = { total_integration_batts = global.EU_total_battalions_var }
	set_temp_variable = { army_xp_pooled = global.EU_army_xp_pool }
	multiply_temp_variable = { total_integration_batts = 10 }
	
	set_temp_variable = { army_percent_temp = army_xp_pooled }
	multiply_temp_variable = { army_percent_temp = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { army_percent_temp = total_integration_batts }
	divide_temp_variable = { army_percent_temp = 10 }
	
	#Find percentage
	set_variable = { global.EU_army_integration_percentage = army_percent_temp }
}

EU_turn_DWV_into_EU = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			AUS_DWV_member = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = EU_FOUNDER }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeeu.1
			days = 1
			random_hours = 72
		}
	}
}

EU_create_EU_not_from_DWV = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = EU_FOUNDER }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeeu.1
			days = 1
			random_hours = 72
		}
	}
}

AUS_lower_all_minorities = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = lower_all_minorities_tt
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.minorities_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
					AUS_is_minority = yes
				}
				THIS_subtract_ten_collapse = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_raise_all_minorities = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = raise_all_minorities_tt
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.minorities_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
					AUS_is_minority = yes
				}
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_change_revolt_progress_to_all_minorities = {
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_variable = revolt_progress_change
			AUS_can_collapse = yes
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = revolt_progress_all_minorities_tt
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.minorities_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
						AUS_is_minority = yes
					}
					THIS = {
						set_temp_variable = { THIS.revolt_progress_change = PREV.revolt_progress_change}
						BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_reduce_collapse_idea = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse
			add_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_2
			add_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_3
			add_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_4 }
		remove_ideas = AUS_legacy_of_collapse_4
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_reduces_collapse
	}
}


AUS_the_state_modifiers = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_local_building_slots_factor = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_local_manpower = -0.40 }
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_local_resources_factor = -0.25 }
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_state_production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_state_production_speed_arms_factory_factor = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { AUS.recently_federalized_state_state_production_speed_dockyard_factor = -0.15 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { region = 21 }
				has_state_flag = default_danubian_state
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_recently_federalized_state }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.240
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

AUS_gleich_add_hungarian_grievance = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_gliech_hungarian_grievance
	add_to_variable = {
		var = HUN.ausgleich_grievances
		value = 1
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = HUN.ausgleich_grievances
					value = 2
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausgleich.55
					days = 2
					random = 120
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausgleich.56
					days = 2
					random = 120
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = HUN.ausgleich_grievances
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausgleich.57
					days = 2
					random = 120
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

CZE_do_revolt = {
	clear_all_relations = yes
	set_country_flag = BOTDE_has_revolted_before
	AUS = {
		country_event = revolt.7 #Notification
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = CZE }
			transfer_state_to = CZE
		}
	}
	CZE = { 
		if = {
			limit = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
			AUS_remove_from_DWV =  yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			CZE = {
				check_variable = { THIS.industrial_stuff_local > 0 }
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { THIS.industrial_stuff_local = 1 }
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		set_global_flag = { flag = CZE_recent_revolt days = 720 value = 1 }
		set_variable = { CZE.subject_revolt_progress = 0 }
	}
}

CRO_do_revolt = {
	CRO = {
		CRO_remove_karl = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = CRO_collapse
		set_country_flag = cro_revolt_in_progress
		clear_all_relations = yes
		if = {
			limit = { MNT = { is_ally_with = AUS } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { is_ally_with = AUS }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			load_oob = CRO_revolution
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { THIS.industrial_stuff_local > 0 } }
			subtract_from_variable = { THIS.industrial_stuff_local = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
			AUS_remove_from_DWV =  yes
		}
	}
	AUS = {
		country_event = revolt.6 #Notification
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CRO
			}
			transfer_state_to = CRO
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		set_global_flag = { flag = CRO_recent_revolt days = 720 value = 1 }
	}
}

		limit = { check_variable = { THIS.industrial_stuff_local > 0 } }

		AUS_remove_from_DWV =  yes
	}
	hidden_effect = {

	}
}

AUS_reset_party_names = {
	if = {
		limit = { AUS_unstable_collapse = yes }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			name = AUS_collapse_totalist_party
			long_name = AUS_collapse_totalist_party_long
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			name = AUS_totalist_party
			long_name = AUS_totalist_party_long
		}
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = syndicalist
		name = AUS_syndicalist_party
		long_name = AUS_syndicalist_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = radical_socialist
		name = AUS_radical_socialist_party
		long_name = AUS_radical_socialist_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = social_democrat
		name = AUS_social_democrat_party
		long_name = AUS_social_democrat_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = social_liberal
		name = AUS_social_liberal_party
		long_name = AUS_social_liberal_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		name = AUS_market_liberal_party
		long_name = AUS_market_liberal_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = social_conservative
		name = AUS_social_conservative_party
		long_name = AUS_social_conservative_party_long
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = authoritarian_democrat
		name = AUS_authoritarian_democrat_party
		long_name = AUS_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			name = AUS_VF_NAME
			long_name = AUS_VF_NAME_LONG
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			name = AUS_paternal_autocrat_party
			long_name = AUS_paternal_autocrat_party_long
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS_unstable_collapse = yes }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			name = AUS_collapse_national_populist_party
			long_name = AUS_collapse_national_populist_party_long
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			name = AUS_national_populist_party
			long_name = AUS_national_populist_party_long
		}
	}
}
AUS_5BW_peace_collapse = {
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_war_with = SER } }
		AUS = { set_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_SER }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_war_with = ROM } }
		AUS = { set_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_ROM }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_SER } }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ally_with = AUS
				has_war_with = SER
				NOT = { tag = FIU }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SKS = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = SER
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = SKS
							is_core_of = SKS
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = SKS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BOS = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = SER
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = BOS
							is_core_of = BOS
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = BOS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SLO = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = SER
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = SLO
							is_core_of = SLO
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = SLO
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = SER
						is_core_of = SER
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = SER
			}
		}
		AUS = { clr_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_SER }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_ROM } }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				has_war_with = ROM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TRS = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = TRS
							is_core_of = TRS
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = TRS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BAN = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = BAN
							is_core_of = BAN
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = BAN
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BUK = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = BUK
							is_core_of = BUK
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = BUK
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = ROM
						is_core_of = ROM
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROM
			}
		}
		AUS = { clr_country_flag = collapse_5bw_war_with_ROM }
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_war_with = SER
			is_in_faction_with = AUS
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					is_subject_of = SER
				}
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = PREV
				message = WHITE_PEACE_MESSAGE_AUS_COLLAPSES_5BW
			}
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_war_with = ROM
			is_in_faction_with = AUS
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROM
					is_subject_of = ROM
				}
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = PREV
				message = WHITE_PEACE_MESSAGE_AUS_COLLAPSES_5BW
			}
		}
	}
	set_global_flag = fifth_balkan_war_ended
	set_global_flag = AUS_collapsed_during_5BW
	AUS_remove_all_SER_state_revolt_target_modifiers = yes
	AUS_remove_all_ROM_state_revolt_target_modifiers = yes
	every_country = {
		limit = { is_ally_with = SER }
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausfor.1070
			hours = 1
		}
	}
	SER = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				CRO = { exists = no }
				check_variable = { CRO.subject_revolt_progress > 0.39 }
				OR = {
					owns_state = 1102
					owns_state = 109
					any_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 1102
							owns_state = 109
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.5
				days = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 1103
				check_variable = { SLO.subject_revolt_progress > 0.49 }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SER_slavic_federation }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.7
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

				exists = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
			}
			var:69.owner = {
				has_country_flag = released_via_austrian_collapse
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = HUN
					tag = CZE
					tag = CRO
					tag = GAL
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = BOH_sudeten_german_divide
					has_idea = BOH_sudeten_german_divide_2
				}
				NOT = { overlord = { tag = AUS } }
			}
		}
		var:69.owner = {
			log = "AUS_collapse_splinter_setup - [?69.GetName] owner: [?69.owner.GetName]"
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.10 #German-Bohemian Secession
				days = 7
				random_hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
	# Galicia Splinters #
	if = {
		limit = {
			WSU = {
				exists = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt }
			}
			var:91.owner = {
				has_country_flag = released_via_austrian_collapse
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = HUN
					tag = CZE
					tag = CRO
					tag = GAL
				}
			}
		}
		var:91.owner = {
			log = "AUS_collapse_splinter_setup - [?91.GetName] owner: [?91.owner.GetName]"
			country_event = {
				id = wsu.1 #West Ukraine Secession
				days = 4
				random_hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
	
	# BUK fired by WSU because battle for lviv
}

AUS_post_collapse_effect = {
	PGU = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.1007
				days = 7
				random_days = 48
			}
		}
	}
	HNZ = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.1010
				days = 7
				random_days = 48
			}
		}
	}
	CZE = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			country_event = {
				id = bdecze.15
				days = 2
				random_days = 58
				random_hours = 240
			}
		}
	}
	WSU = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				UKR = { exists = yes }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = constituents.700
				days = 2
				random_hours = 192
			}
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = SER }
					OR = {
						AND = {
							tag = MNT
							has_country_flag = MNT_released_in_austrian_collapse
						}
						tag = SKS
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROM }
					OR = {
						tag = BUK
						tag = TRS
					}
				}
				AND = {
					tag = SLO
					NOT = { is_guaranteed_by = AUS }
				}
			}
			exists = yes
		}
		country_event = constituents.999
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_borderwars_flag }
		clr_country_flag = AUS_borderwars_flag
	}
}

do_minority_revolt_setup = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			REV = {
				is_subject = yes
				overlord = { AUS_is_constituent = yes }
			}
		}
		OVERLORD = {
			THIS_add_five_collapse = yes
			end_puppet = PREV
			PREV = {
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				every_state = { teleport_armies = { to_state_array = owned_states } }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
		RVO = { clr_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner }
	}
	else = {
		do_minority_revolt_basic = yes
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = no_4_months } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = 4_months_to_win
	}
	if = {
		limit = { REV = { AUS_DWV_member = yes } }
		AUS_remove_from_DWV =  yes
	}
	remove_ideas = {
		AUS_part_of_the_Empire
		AUS_transleithanian_sphere
		AUS_cisleithanian_sphere
	}
}

do_minority_revolt_basic = {
	clr_global_flag = no_4_months
	if = {
		limit = { REV = { tag = BOS } } #exception so bosnia doesn't get nearly all of SKS's states if they revolt first
		every_core_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = RVO
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = SKS
					has_state_flag = solid_state
				}
			}
			REV = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	else = {
		every_core_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = RVO
				#Exceptions
				NOT = {
					is_szekler = yes
					has_state_flag = solid_state
					AND = {
						state = 875
						REV = { tag = BAN }
					}
				}
			}
			REV = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_event_target = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag } }
			REV = {
				set_country_flag = BOTDE_in_revolt
				country_event = {
					id = revolt_peace.0
					days = 124
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { REV = { has_country_flag = SLO_CRO_sponsored_revolt } }
		SLO_CRO_sponsored_revolt_effect = yes
	}
	else = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RVO
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	REV = {
		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt
		set_variable = { REV.subject_revolt_progress = 0 }
		REV_spawn_units = yes
	}
	RVO = {
		THIS_add_five_collapse = yes
		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
	}
	clear_global_event_target = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
}

REV_spawn_units = {
	if = {
		limit = { tag = SLO }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Pehotne Divizije" } }
			division_template = {
				name = "Pehotne Divizije"
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }

				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Milica" } }
			division_template = {
				name = "Milica"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }

					militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }

					militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = num_owned_states
			random_owned_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Milica\" division_template = \"Milica\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					33 = {
						create_unit = {

						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = num_owned_states
			random_owned_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Miliz\" division_template = \"Miliz\" start_experience_factor = 0.4" 
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					33 = {
						create_unit = { 
							division = "name = \"Infanteriedivision\" division_template = \"Infanteriedivision\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" 
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
					67 = {}
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Infanteriedivision\" division_template = \"Infanteriedivision\" start_experience_factor = 0.2" 
				owner = PREV
				count = 3
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { PREV.paramilitary_value > 0 } }
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Infanteriedivision\" division_template = \"Infanteriedivision\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
					count = PREV.paramilitary_value
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}

do_minority_rise = {
	if = {
		limit = { var:capital_scope.owner = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus } }
		THIS = { 
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.002 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
	}
	else = {
		THIS = { 
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.01 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
	}
}

do_minority_rise_advanced_calc = {
	AUS_average_state_resistance = yes
	set_temp_variable = { additional_value = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { subtractive_value = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { nationalist_value = THIS.paramilitary_value } #Paramilitaries
	set_temp_variable = { collapse_value_AUS = AUS.subject_revolt_progress }
	set_temp_variable = { resistance_value = THIS.avg_resistance }
	set_temp_variable = { minority_cores = THIS.num_core_states }
	divide_temp_variable = { minority_cores = 160 } # 100 * 16
	THIS = {
		capital_scope = {
			owner = {
				PREV.PREV = { #Owner of current capital; e.g. Hungary for Slovakia
					set_temp_variable = { collapse_value_owner = THIS.subject_revolt_progress }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { NOT = { has_idea = AUS_unsupported_rebels } } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = 0.0075 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { subtractive_value = AUS.stability }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { subtractive_value = 0.5 } #If below 50% stability, get a malus
	divide_temp_variable = { subtractive_value = 20 }
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_war = yes } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { subtractive_value = 0.02 }
	}
	divide_temp_variable = { nationalist_value = 3 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { collapse_value_owner = 1.75 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = collapse_value_AUS }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = nationalist_value }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = collapse_value_owner }
	divide_temp_variable = { additional_value = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { resistance_value = 1600 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = minority_cores }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = global.extra_value_war_exhaust }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = THIS.extra_value }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = global.extra_collapse_federalizing }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = modifier@BOTDE_revolt_rate_modifier }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { additional_value = subtractive_value }
	add_to_temp_variable = { additional_value = resistance_value }
	multiply_temp_variable = { additional_value = 0.8 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = additional_value }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change < 1 } } #for modifier tooltips
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: do_minority_rise_advanced_calc: [?revolt_progress_change]"
		BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
	}
}

AUS_do_schizo_test = {
	var:schizophrenic = {
		set_temp_variable = { collapse = THIS.subject_revolt_progress }
	}
	
	set_temp_variable = { schizo_value = global.schizo_value_var }
	
	set_temp_variable = { calculator = 0 }
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { calculator = collapse }
	add_to_temp_variable = { calculator = schizo_value }

	
	set_variable = {
		var = global.schizocalc
		value = calculator
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = schizocalc
				value = 0.96
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = no_schizo
	}
}

			#}

			set_variable = { global.BOTDE_picker_maxval = 5 }
		}
		2 = { #Strategy Shaker
			set_variable = { global.BOTDE_randomevent_AUS_picker = 4 }
			set_variable = { global.BOTDE_picker_maxval = 2 }
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_event_roulette_lets_go_gambling = { 
	AUS_picker_select_event_type = yes
	BOTDE_roulette_nationselect = yes
	BOTDE_numpicker = yes
	
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: BOTDE_event_roulette_lets_go_gambling: Austrian Collapse Event roulette rolled event ethnic.[?global.BOTDE_event_target]_[?global.BOTDE_randomevent_AUS_picker]_[?global.BOTDE_picker] with maximum roll value of [?global.BOTDE_picker_maxval]"
	
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			country_event = {
				id = ethnic.[foci]_[type]_[num] #For example, a basic event for Austria with a random value of 1 should be: ETHNIC.1_1_2. The 2nd mission for Bohemia should be ethnic.3_2_2.
			}
		}
		foci = "[?global.BOTDE_event_target]" #What tag is getting an event.
		type = "[?global.BOTDE_randomevent_AUS_picker]" #Type of event. Basic? Mission? Minority? Stratshaker?
		num = "[?global.BOTDE_picker]" #Event number.
	}
	clear_variable = global.BOTDE_event_target
	clear_variable = global.BOTDE_picker_maxval
	clear_variable = global.BOTDE_randomevent_AUS_picker
	clear_variable = global.BOTDE_picker
}
BOTDE_roulette_nationselect = {
	random_list = {
		60 = { #Select an event about Austria
			set_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 1 }
		}
		40 = { #Select an event about the constituents (Constituents will get their own reel of events)
			random_list = {
				40 = { #Hungary
					set_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 2 }
				}
				60 = { #Not Hungary, Bohemia is 3, Illyria is 4, and Galicia is 5
					set_variable_to_random = {
						var = global.BOTDE_event_target
						min = 3
						max = 5
						integer = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { BOTDE_randomevent_AUS_picker = 3 } }
				}
				divide_variable = { global.BOTDE_picker_maxval = 2 }
				round_variable = global.BOTDE_picker_maxval
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #check if the const isn't a const anymore
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 2 }
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = HUN
						NOT = { owns_state = 43 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 3 }
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = CZE
						NOT = { owns_state = 1129 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 4 }
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = CRO
						NOT = { owns_state = 109 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 5 }
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = GAL
						NOT = { owns_state = 91 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.BOTDE_event_target = 1 }
	}
}
BOTDE_numpicker = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_variable_to_random = {
				var = global.BOTDE_picker
				min = 1
				max = [max]
				integer = yes
			}
		}
		max = "[?global.BOTDE_picker_maxval]"
	}
}

#### PICKER LOGIC: AUSTRIA
#BASIC EVENTS: 20. 20 basic event (with different effects each): 1-6 negligible, 7-16 moderate, 17-20 severe. 2 multi-choice for negligible. 5 multi-choice for moderate. 2 multi-choice for severe. of these, 1 of each are three-choices.
#MISSIONS: 8. 8 diff missions: 2 easy, 2 hard, 4 medium 
#PARAMILITARY: 1. DEPRECATED
#STRATSHAKER: 4. 4 different strategy shakers. Strat shaker is a misc thing
#CONSTITUENT: 8 PER CONSTITUENT. 8 events per constituent. 4 two-choice and one three-choice. If a constituent is gone and this script selects that constituent, it will run AUS_picker_AUS. This is the same script but only including Austria. 1-2 minor. 7-8 major.
#2 = Hungary. 3 = Bohemia. 4 = Illyria. 5 = Galicia.
#### PICKER LOGIC: CONSTITUENT.
#BASIC EVENTS: 15.
#MISSIONS: 4.

#MINORITY: 5 PER MINORITY. 5 events per minority. 2 two-choice. 1 minor. 1 major. 3 moderate.
#6. Slovenia. 7. Slovakia. 8. Transylvania. 9. Banat. 10. Bukovina. 11. Bosnia. 12. Montenegro. 13. West Ukraine. 14. Krakow. 15. Carpatho-Ukraine. 16. Burgenland. 17. German-Bohemia. 18. Venice. 19. Srpska.
#Minorities are type 3 event.

AUS_average_state_resistance = {
	clear_temp_array = global.temp_states
	clear_variable = THIS.avg_resistance
	set_temp_variable = { global.num_states = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { global.resistance_sum = 0 }
	set_variable = { THIS.avg_resistance = 0 }
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = PREV
			has_resistance = yes
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { global.temp_states = THIS }
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.temp_states
		add_to_temp_variable = { global.num_states = 1 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { global.resistance_sum = THIS.resistance }
	}
	divide_temp_variable = { global.resistance_sum = global.num_states }
	set_variable = { THIS.avg_resistance = global.resistance_sum }
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = BOTDE_avg_resistance_target }
		clear_global_event_target = BOTDE_avg_resistance_target
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = BOTDE_avg_resistance_owner }
		clear_global_event_target = BOTDE_avg_resistance_owner
	}
}

BOTDE_minority_test = {
	do_minority_rise = yes
	do_minority_rise_advanced_calc = yes
}
