AUS_divide_hungary_effect = {
	HUN = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SVK
				NOT = {
					state = 1122
					state = 1136
				}
			}
			SVK = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = CPU }
			CPU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BAN
				NOT = { state = 45 }
			}
			BAN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = TRS }
			transfer_state_to = TRS
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
			OR = {
				tag = TRS
				tag = CPU
				tag = SVK
				tag = BAN
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_transleithania
			}
		}
		BOTDE_create_austrian_emperor = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_30 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { AUS_DWV_member = yes } }
			AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research } }
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TRS }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRS_kingdom
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_display_on_gui_even_if_it_exists
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = BAN }
			set_cosmetic_tag = BAN_kingdom
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_display_on_gui_even_if_it_exists
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CPU }
			set_cosmetic_tag = CPU_kingdom
		}
		add_ideas = {
			AUS_part_of_the_Empire
			AUS_transleithanian_sphere
		}
	}
}

AUS_restore_bosnia_condominium_effect = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			AUS_state_is_owned_by_aus_or_subjects = yes
			NOT = {
				is_owned_by = MNT
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = BOS
				is_core_of = MNT
				state = 163
				state = 1098
				state = 1270
			}
		}
		
		BOS = {
			transfer_state = PREV
			AUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = botde_constituent
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = CONST_proper
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
				}
				set_popularities = {
					totalist = 0
					radical_socialist = 0
					syndicalist = 2
					social_democrat = 4
					social_liberal = 6
					market_liberal = 8
					social_conservative = 41
					authoritarian_democrat = 12
					paternal_autocrat = 19
					national_populist = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = { has_variable = THIS.temp_this_population }
		clear_variable = THIS.temp_this_population
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = { has_variable = THIS.temp_divisor }
		clear_variable = THIS.temp_divisor
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_array^num < 1 } }
		add_to_temp_array = { temp_array = ROOT }
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = temp_array
		set_variable = { THIS.temp_this_population = max_manpower_k }
		multiply_variable = { THIS.temp_this_population = 1000 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_population = THIS.temp_this_population }
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = temp_array
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
		set_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

		set_variable = { THIS.temp_divisor = THIS.temp_this_population }
		divide_variable = { THIS.temp_divisor = temp_population }

		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_totalist = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_syndicalist = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_radical_socialist = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_democrat = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_liberal = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_market_liberal = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_social_conservative = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_authoritarian_democrat = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_paternal_autocrat = THIS.temp_divisor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { undivided_temp_national_populist = THIS.temp_divisor }

		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_totalist = undivided_temp_totalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_syndicalist = undivided_temp_syndicalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_radical_socialist = undivided_temp_radical_socialist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_social_democrat = undivided_temp_social_democrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_social_liberal = undivided_temp_social_liberal }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_market_liberal = undivided_temp_market_liberal }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_social_conservative = undivided_temp_social_conservative }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_authoritarian_democrat = undivided_temp_authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_paternal_autocrat = undivided_temp_paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_national_populist = undivided_temp_national_populist }

		log = "AUS_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect: [THIS.GetName] - in temp_array, temp_divisor: [?THIS.temp_divisor], temp_population: [?temp_population], temp_this_population [?THIS.temp_this_population], totalist: [?party_popularity_100@totalist], syndicalist: [?party_popularity_100@syndicalist], radical_socialist: [?party_popularity_100@radical_socialist], social_democrat: [?party_popularity_100@social_democrat], social_liberal: [?party_popularity_100@social_liberal], market_liberal: [?party_popularity_100@market_liberal], social_conservative: [?party_popularity_100@social_conservative], authoritarian_democrat: [?party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat], paternal_autocrat: [?party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat], national_populist: [?party_popularity_100@national_populist]"
	}
	log = "AUS_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect: totalist: [?temp_totalist], syndicalist: [?temp_syndicalist], radical_socialist: [?temp_radical_socialist], social_democrat: [?temp_social_democrat], social_liberal: [?temp_social_liberal], market_liberal: [?temp_market_liberal], social_conservative: [?temp_social_conservative], authoritarian_democrat: [?temp_authoritarian_democrat], paternal_autocrat: [?temp_paternal_autocrat], national_populist: [?temp_national_populist]"
}

AUS_apply_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = {
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = totalist
	    popularity = temp_totalist
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = syndicalist
	    popularity = temp_syndicalist
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = radical_socialist
	    popularity = temp_radical_socialist
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = social_democrat
	    popularity = temp_social_democrat
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = social_liberal
	    popularity = temp_social_liberal
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = market_liberal
	    popularity = temp_market_liberal
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = social_conservative
	    popularity = temp_social_conservative
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = authoritarian_democrat
	    popularity = temp_authoritarian_democrat
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = paternal_autocrat
	    popularity = temp_paternal_autocrat
	}
	set_political_party = {
	    ideology = national_populist
	    popularity = temp_national_populist
	}
}

AUS_annex_const_effect = {
	effect_tooltip = {
		AUS = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { do_not_do_party_pop_calc < 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { temp_array = THIS } } }
				add_to_temp_array  = { temp_array = THIS }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { temp_array = AUS } } }
				add_to_temp_array  = { temp_array = AUS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
			AUS_remove_from_DWV = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea }
			remove_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = HUN }
			every_unit_leader = { add_trait = { trait = BOTDE_HUN_unit_trait } }
			every_scientist = { add_scientist_trait = BOTDE_HUN_scientist_trait }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress < 0.11 } }
				set_country_flag = AUS_collapse_HUN_stays
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CZE }
			every_unit_leader = { add_trait = { trait = BOTDE_CZE_unit_trait } }
			every_scientist = { add_scientist_trait = BOTDE_CZE_scientist_trait }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CRO }
			every_unit_leader = { add_trait = { trait = BOTDE_CRO_unit_trait } }
			every_scientist = { add_scientist_trait = BOTDE_CRO_scientist_trait }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GAL }
			every_unit_leader = { add_trait = { trait = BOTDE_GAL_unit_trait } }
			every_scientist = { add_scientist_trait = BOTDE_GAL_scientist_trait }
		}
		every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = AUS }
		every_scientist = { set_nationality = AUS }
		every_core_state = { add_core_of = AUS }
		every_subject_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					overlord = { AUS_is_constituent = yes }
					NOT = {
						has_autonomy_state = botde_fiume
						NOT = { has_global_flag = AUS_annexed_fiume }
					}
				}
				AUS = {
					transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
					transfer_int_upgrade = yes
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { do_not_do_party_pop_calc < 1 } }
						add_to_temp_array  = { temp_array = PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { PREV = { is_ai = no } }
						change_tag_from = PREV.PREV
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
				get_current_government_type = yes
				if = {
					limit = { tag = FIU }
					AUS = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = botde_fiume
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						AUS_is_danubian_tag = yes
						NOT = { tag = FIU }
					}
					AUS = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = botde_constituent
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomy_state = kr_default_puppet
					}
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = AUS_transleithanian_sphere }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = AUS_transleithanian_sphere
						add_idea = AUS_cisleithanian_sphere
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = AUS_transleithanian_sphere_fiume }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = AUS_transleithanian_sphere_fiume
						add_idea = AUS_cisleithanian_sphere_fiume
					}
				}
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			transfer_int_upgrade = yes
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { do_not_do_party_pop_calc < 1 } }
				AUS_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = yes
				AUS_apply_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { is_ai = no } }
				change_tag_from = PREV.PREV
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS } }
			remove_from_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS }
		}
	}
}

AUS_federalize_effect = {
	set_global_flag = AUS_federalized
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.AUS_all_possible_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				THIS = { AUS_is_constituent = yes }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						tag = HUN
						NOT = { 
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania_minorities
						}
					}
					tag = ALA
					tag = ENG
				}
			}
			add_to_temp_array  = { temp_array = THIS }
		}
	}
	AUS = { AUS_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = yes }
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.AUS_all_possible_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				THIS = { AUS_is_constituent = yes }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						tag = HUN
						NOT = { 
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania_minorities
						}
					}
					tag = AUS
					tag = ALA
					tag = ENG
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { do_not_do_party_pop_calc = 1 }
			AUS_annex_const_effect = yes
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = BRG_selected_LIC_prince
				ENG = { is_subject_of = AUS }
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ENG
					autonomy_state = botde_constituent_color_overload
				}
			}
		}
		add_manpower = 300000
		set_stability = 0.5
		set_war_support = 0.5
		news_event = {
			id = bdeausnews.2
			hours = 12
			random_hours = 24
		}
		AUS_apply_average_party_pop_of_countries_effect = yes
	}
}

AUS_federalize_trialist_effect = {
	AUS_federalize_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { CRO = { has_country_flag = trialist_extra } }
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_trialism_illyria
	}
	if = {
		limit = { CZE = { has_country_flag = trialist_extra } }
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_trialism_bohemia
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = trialist_extra } }
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_trialism_britain
	}
}

AUS_do_fed_name = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_social_democrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = KX_POLICEMAN_SWEAR_TO_GOD }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_FUN_social_democrat
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_social_liberal
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = KX_POLICEMAN_SWEAR_TO_GOD }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_FUN_social_liberal
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				AND = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_VF_WON }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hungary }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_AHE
		}
		else = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_social_conservative
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KX_POLICEMAN_SWEAR_TO_GOD }
				set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_FUN_social_conservative
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_country_flag = AUS_VF_WON
				}
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_karl_absolute }
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_paternal_autocrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = KX_POLICEMAN_SWEAR_TO_GOD }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_FUN_paternal_autocrat
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_karl_absolute }
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_federalized_tag_authoritarian_democrat
	}
}

SKS_revolt_units_SER = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Četnici" } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Četnici"
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Četnička milicija" } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Četnička milicija"
			regiments = {
				militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 4
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Četnici\" division_template = \"Četnici\" start_experience_factor = 0.4" 
				owner = SKS
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 8
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Četnička milicija\" division_template = \"Četnička milicija\" start_experience_factor = 0.4" 
				owner = SKS
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { extra_divs_temp = THIS.paramilitary_value }
	multiply_temp_variable  = { extra_divs_temp = 1.5 }
	round_temp_variable = extra_divs_temp
	add_to_temp_variable = { extra_divs_temp = THIS.extra_divs_meme }
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: SKS_revolt_units_SER: THIS.extra_divs_temp: [?THIS.extra_divs_temp]"
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = { check_variable = { THIS.extra_divs_temp > 0 } }
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Četnici\" division_template = \"Četnici\" start_experience_factor = 0.2" 
				owner = PREV
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { THIS.extra_divs_temp = 1 }
	}
}

				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Militia Frătiei" } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Militia Frătiei"
			regiments = {
				militia= { x = 0 y = 0 }
				militia= { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia= { x = 0 y = 2 }
				militia= { x = 1 y = 0 }
				militia= { x = 1 y = 1 }
				militia= { x = 1 y = 2 }
				militia= { x = 2 y = 0 }
				militia= { x = 2 y = 1 }
				militia= { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 6
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Legiunea Frătiei\" division_template = \"Legiunea Frătiei\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
				owner = PREV
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 8
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Militia Frătiei\" division_template = \"Militia Frătiei\" start_experience_factor = 0.4" 
				owner = PREV
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { extra_divs_temp = THIS.paramilitary_value }
	multiply_temp_variable  = { extra_divs_temp = 1.5 }
	round_temp_variable = extra_divs_temp
	add_to_temp_variable = { extra_divs_temp = THIS.extra_divs_meme }
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: TRS_revolt_units_ROM: THIS.extra_divs_temp: [?THIS.extra_divs_temp]"
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = { check_variable = { THIS.extra_divs_temp > 0 } }
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Legiunea Frătiei\" division_template = \"Legiunea Frătiei\" start_experience_factor = 0.2" 
				owner = PREV
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { THIS.extra_divs_temp = 1 }
	}
}

AUS_tally_ausgleich = { #-1 successes - Hungarian revolt. 0-2 successes - bad. 3-5 successes - meh. 6+ successes - good.
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = -1
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_terrible_ausgleich
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 0
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 2
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_bad_ausgleich
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 3
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 5
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_meh_ausgleich
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 6
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_good_ausgleich
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania_minorities
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausgleich.59
			days = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_status_quo_1927
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausgleich.71
			days = 3
		}
	}
	country_event = {
		id = bdeausgleich.58
		days = 3
	}
}

BOTDE_minority_pulse_test = {
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = ROOT.austria_minority_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_ongoing
						has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_peoples
					}
					has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
					has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_minority_focus
				}
			}
			do_minority_rise = yes
			do_minority_rise_advanced_calc = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.999 }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_temp
						has_global_flag = recent_minority_revolt
						has_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
						has_country_flag = BOTDE_revolt_hold
						AND = {
							tag = MNT
							exists = yes
						}
					}
				}
				all_other_country = {
					limit = { is_in_array = { ROOT.austria_minority_array = THIS } }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt }
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_temp
			THIS = {
				save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt
				set_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt
				#country_event = revolt.10
				capital_scope = {
					owner = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "AUS_minor_imminent_revolt"
						save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
						set_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
						activate_mission = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_headsup
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "AUS_minor_imminent_revolt"
				activate_mission = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_headsup
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope.owner = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus } }
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = -0.005 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_minority_focus }
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = -0.025 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BOTDE_revolt_hold
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.94 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt }
			}
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
				OR = {
					AND = {
						var:THIS.capital_scope.owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus } }
						check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.75 }
					}
					AND = {
						var:THIS.capital_scope.owner = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }
						check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.85 }
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_minority_test_for_revolt_extra = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BOTDE_revolt_hold
			check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.94 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt }
		}
		set_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
			OR = {
				AND = {
					var:THIS.capital_scope.owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus } }
					check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.75 }
				}
				AND = {
					var:THIS.capital_scope.owner = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }
					check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.85 }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
	}
}

BOTDE_5BW_peace = {
	
	for_each_scope_loop = { #Array for all participating Belgrade Pact tags fighting against Austria
		array = global.AUS_5BW_BP_array
		log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.AUS_5BW_BP_array"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
			log = "[THIS.GetName] adding to array global.fucked_capped_5bw"
			add_to_temp_array = { array = global.fucked_capped_5bw }
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = AUS
				}
				add_to_temp_array = { array = global.fucked_capped_5bw }
			}
			else = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = PREV
						}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = PREV
							is_claimed_by = PREV
							if = {
								limit = {
									PREV = { tag = SER }
								}
								OR = {
									is_core_of = BOS
									is_core_of = SKS
								}
							}
						}
						AUS_state_is_owned_by_aus_or_subjects = yes
					}
					owner = { #Denote state owner and save
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									is_in_array = { global.5bw_AH_rereceive = THIS }
								}
							}
							add_to_temp_array = { global.5bw_AH_rereceive = THIS }
							log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.5bw_AH_rereceive"
						}
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { global.BW_GAINZ = THIS }
					PREV = {
						transfer_state = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.BW_GAINZ
		log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.BW_GAINZ"
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BAN
				BAN = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROM
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = TRS
				}
			}
			BAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUK
				BUK = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROM
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = TRS
				}
			}
			BUK = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRS
				TRS = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROM
						is_subject_of = ROM
					}
				}
			}
			TRS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROM
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ROM
					is_claimed_by = ROM
				}
			}
			ROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SKS
				SKS = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SER
						is_subject_of = SER
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = BOS
				}
			}
			SKS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BOS
				BOS = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SER
						is_subject_of = SER
					}
				}
			}
			BOS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MNT
			}
			MNT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = SER
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SER
					is_claimed_by = SER
				}
			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				save_event_target_as = BW_GAINZER
			}
			
		}
	}
	
	for_each_scope_loop = { #Return exclaves to original owner
		array = global.5bw_AH_rereceive
		log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.5bw_AH_rereceive"
		save_event_target_as = AH_rereceiver
		event_target:BW_GAINZER = {
			log = "[THIS.GetName] is event target BW_GAINZER"
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { global.BW_GAINZ = THIS }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:AH_rereceiver
						is_claimed_by = event_target:AH_rereceiver
					}
					NOT = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_owned_by = TRS
									is_owned_by = BAN
									is_owned_by = BUK
								}
							}
							PREV = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROM }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_owned_by = SKS
									is_owned_by = BOS
									is_owned_by = MNT
								}
							}
							PREV = { is_owner_neighbor_of = SER }
						}
					}
				}
				log = "[THIS.GetName] returning to previous owner"
				event_target:AH_rereceiver = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	for_each_scope_loop = { #Annex all capped subjects into capital controller, AUS if the nation is a subject of it
		array = global.fucked_capped_5bw
		log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.fucked_capped_5bw"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MNT
					tag = SKS
				}
				CRO = { is_in_faction_with = AUS has_war_together_with = AUS }
			}
			CRO = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = SER }
			AUS = { AUS_occupy_SER_effect = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = TRS
					tag = BAN
				}
				HUN = { is_in_faction_with = AUS has_war_together_with = AUS }
			}
			HUN = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUK
				GAL = { is_in_faction_with = AUS has_war_together_with = AUS }
			}
			GAL = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ROM }
			if = {
				limit = { UKR = { is_in_faction_with = AUS } }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = UKR }
					transfer_state_to = UKR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BUL = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = AUS
							has_war_with = ROM
						}
						NOT = { has_war_with = AUS }
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = BUL }
					transfer_state_to = BUL
				}
			}
			AUS = { AUS_occupy_ROM_effect = yes }
		}
		else = {
			AUS = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_5BW_init = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = SER
				tag = ROM
				tag = SKS
				tag = TRS
				tag = BOS
				tag = BAN
				tag = BUK
				tag = MNT
				tag = GRE
			}
			has_war_with = AUS
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = 5BW_BP
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.AUS_5BW_BP_array
		}
	}
	
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = SER
				has_war_with = ROM
			}
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = 5BW_AH
		log = "[THIS.GetName] on array global.AUS_5BW_AH_array"
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.AUS_5BW_AH_array
		}
	}
}

BOTDE_5BW_looping_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { SER = { is_ai = yes } }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SKS
					tag = BOS
					tag = MNT
				}
				has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
					has_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
					has_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
				}
				exists = no
			}
			THIS = {
				set_country_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_start
				set_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
				save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
			}
			set_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
			set_global_flag = no_4_months
			SER = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
				activate_mission = SER_revolt_mission
			}
			AUS = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
				activate_mission = AUS_SER_revolt_mission
			}
			CRO = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
				activate_mission = AUS_SER_revolt_mission
			}
			SKS = {
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = THIS.extra_divs
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
			}
			BOS = {
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = THIS.extra_divs
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	if = {
		limit = { ROM = { is_ai = yes } }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = TRS
					tag = BAN
					tag = BUK
				}
				has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
					has_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
					has_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
				}
				exists = no
			}
			
			THIS = {
				set_country_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_start
				set_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
				save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
			}
			set_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
			set_global_flag = no_4_months
			ROM = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
				activate_mission = ROM_revolt_mission
			}
			AUS = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
				activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
			}
			if = {
				limit = { THIS = { tag = BUK } }
				GAL = {
					scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
					activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
				}
			}
			else = {
				HUN = {
					scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
					activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
				}
			}
			TRS = {
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = THIS.extra_divs
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
			}
			BAN = {
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = THIS.extra_divs
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
			}
			BUK = {
				THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = THIS.extra_divs
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	country_event = {
		id = bdeausfor.102
		days = 5
	}
	add_to_variable = { global.holyfuckimcumminglois = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { casualties_k > 200 }
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausflavor.140
			days = 3
			random_days = 14
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.holyfuckimcumminglois = 120 } }
		SER = { country_event = bdeausfor.100 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			CRO = {
				surrender_progress > 0.75
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = AUS_CRO_no_5BW_mandate }
		}
		AUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.169
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_szekler_sztuff }
		clr_country_flag = AUS_szekler_sztuff
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_leave_BP_on_5BW_end }
		country_event = {
			id = botdepact.21
			days = 1
			random_hours = 72
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_5BW_240_days_flag }
		clr_global_flag = BOTDE_5BW_240_days_flag
	}
}

AUS_RUS_do_oil_upgrade = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = RUS
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = AUS.AUS_RUS_base_fuel_gain
			value = 300
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = AUS.AUS_RUS_production_oil_factor
			value = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = AUS.AUS_RUS_fuel_gain_factor
			value = 0.04
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = AUS
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = RUS.AUS_RUS_base_fuel_gain
			value = 400
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = RUS.AUS_RUS_production_oil_factor
			value = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = RUS.AUS_RUS_fuel_gain_factor
			value = 0.04
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		var = global.AUS_RUS_max_refineries
		value = 2
	}
}

AUS_become_constituent = {
	add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS }
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.minorities_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.minorities_array = THIS }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.austria_minority_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.austria_minority_array = THIS }
	}
	set_country_flag = CONST_proper
	clr_country_flag = CONST_minor
}

AUS_remove_constituent = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.minorities_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.minorities_array = THIS }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.austria_minority_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.austria_minority_array = THIS }
	}
	clr_country_flag = CONST_proper
	clr_country_flag = CONST_minor
}

AUS_become_minority = {
	add_to_array = { global.minorities_array = THIS }
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS } }
		remove_from_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS }
	}
	set_country_flag = CONST_minor
	clr_country_flag = CONST_proper
}

FifthBW_subject_transfer_control = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_faction_with = SKS
		}
		SKS = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = SER
					}
				}
				SER = {
					set_state_controller = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_faction_with = BOS
		}
		BOS = {
			every_controlled_state = {

					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
						is_core_of = PREV

					owner = {
						has_war_with = ROM
					}

					set_state_controller = PREV
				}
			}
		}

	if = {

			is_in_faction_with = BAN
		}
		BAN = {

				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = ROM
					}
				}
				ROM = {
					set_state_controller = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROM = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = SER
						is_core_of = SER
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = ROM
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_owned_by = ROM
					}
				}
				SER = {
					set_state_controller = PREV
				}

		}

				is_ai = yes

					NOT = {

					}

					set_state_controller = PREV
				}

		}

EUU_avg_political_parties = {
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_totalist= 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_syndicalist = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_radical_socialist = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_democrat = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_liberal = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_market_liberal = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_conservative = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_national_populist = 0 }
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = EUU.EUU_EU_members
		
		set_temp_variable = { totalist_pop = party_popularity@totalist }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_totalist = totalist_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { syndicalist_pop = party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_syndicalist = syndicalist_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { radical_socialist_pop = party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_radical_socialist = radical_socialist_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { social_democrat_pop = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_democrat = social_democrat_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { social_liberal_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_liberal = social_liberal_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { market_liberal_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_market_liberal = market_liberal_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { social_conservative_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_conservative = social_conservative_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { authoritarian_democrat_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_variable = {global.EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat = authoritarian_democrat_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { paternal_autocrat_pop = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat = paternal_autocrat_pop }

		set_temp_variable = { national_populist_pop = party_popularity@national_populist }
		add_to_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_national_populist = national_populist_pop }
	}
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_totalist = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_syndicalist = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num } 
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_radical_socialist = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_democrat = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_liberal = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_market_liberal = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_social_conservative = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }
	divide_variable = { global.EU_party_averages_national_populist = EUU.EUU_EU_members^num }

	log = "EUU_avg_political_parties: EU_party_averages_totalist ([?global.EU_party_averages_totalist]) EU_party_averages_syndicalist ([?global.EU_party_averages_syndicalist]) EU_party_averages_radical_socialist ([?global.EU_party_averages_radical_socialist]) EU_party_averages_social_democrat ([?global.EU_party_averages_social_democrat]) EU_party_averages_social_liberal ([?global.EU_party_averages_social_liberal]) EU_party_averages_market_liberal ([?global.EU_party_averages_market_liberal]) EU_party_averages_social_conservative ([?global.EU_party_averages_social_conservative]) EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat ([?global.EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat]) EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat ([?global.EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat]) EU_party_averages_national_populist ([?global.EU_party_averages_national_populist])"
}

EU_create_pie_chart = {
	EUU_avg_political_parties = yes
	clear_array = pie_chart
	resize_array = {
		array = pie_chart
		value = 8 # 8 is value for authoritarian_democrat frame, so we don't have to make a loop for it
		size = 100 # 100 pieces, each percent is one piece
	}
	set_temp_variable = { authoritarian_democrat_pop = global.EU_party_averages_authoritarian_democrat }
	multiply_temp_variable = { authoritarian_democrat_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = authoritarian_democrat_pop

	set_temp_variable = { totalist_pop = global.EU_party_averages_totalist }
	multiply_temp_variable = { totalist_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = totalist_pop 
	set_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = authoritarian_democrat_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { totalist_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = totalist_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { syndicalist_pop = global.EU_party_averages_syndicalist }
	multiply_temp_variable = { syndicalist_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = syndicalist_pop 
	add_to_temp_variable = { syndicalist_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = syndicalist_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { radical_socialist_pop = global.EU_party_averages_radical_socialist }
	multiply_temp_variable = { radical_socialist_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = radical_socialist_pop 
	add_to_temp_variable = { radical_socialist_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = radical_socialist_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { social_democrat_pop = global.EU_party_averages_social_democrat }
	multiply_temp_variable = { social_democrat_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = social_democrat_pop 
	add_to_temp_variable = { social_democrat_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = social_democrat_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 4 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { social_liberal_pop = global.EU_party_averages_social_liberal }
	multiply_temp_variable = { social_liberal_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = social_liberal_pop
	add_to_temp_variable = { social_liberal_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = social_liberal_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 5 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}
	
	set_temp_variable = { market_liberal_pop = global.EU_party_averages_market_liberal }
	multiply_temp_variable = { market_liberal_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = market_liberal_pop
	add_to_temp_variable = { market_liberal_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = market_liberal_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 6 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}
	
	set_temp_variable = { social_conservative_pop = global.EU_party_averages_social_conservative }
	multiply_temp_variable = { social_conservative_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = social_conservative_pop
	add_to_temp_variable = { social_conservative_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = social_conservative_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 7 }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.last_idx = 1 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { paternal_autocrat_pop = global.EU_party_averages_paternal_autocrat }
	multiply_temp_variable = { paternal_autocrat_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = paternal_autocrat_pop 
	add_to_temp_variable = { paternal_autocrat_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = paternal_autocrat_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 9 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { national_populist_pop = global.EU_party_averages_national_populist }
	multiply_temp_variable = { national_populist_pop = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = national_populist_pop 
	add_to_temp_variable = { national_populist_pop = ROOT.last_idx }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = ROOT.last_idx
		end = national_populist_pop
		set_variable = { pie_chart^v = 10 }
	}

	clear_variable = ROOT.last_idx
	add_to_variable = { pie_chart_dirty = 1 }
}

EUU_subtract_one_pressure_counter = {
	add_to_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = -1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}
EUU_subtract_ten_pressure_counter = {
	add_to_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = -10 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}

	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}

	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}

	add_to_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = 1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}
EUU_add_ten_pressure_counter = {
	add_to_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = 10 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}
EUU_add_hundred_pressure_counter = {
	add_to_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = 100 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}
EUU_add_thousand_pressure_counter = {

	clamp_variable = {
		var = EUM.influence_to_add
		min = 0
	}
	EUU_insurance = yes
}

EUU_add_pressure_to_nation = {
	add_to_variable = { EUM.EU_pressure = EUM.influence_to_add }
	subtract_from_variable = { global.EU_pressure_value = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = 0 }
	EUU_close_influence_menu = yes
	EUU_insurance = yes
}

EUU_close_influence_menu = {
	set_variable = { EUM.influence_to_add = 0 }
	clr_country_flag = EUU_influence_menu_open
	event_target:EUU_influence_target = {
		clr_country_flag = EUM_flag
	}
	clear_global_event_target = EUU_influence_target
}

EUU_insurance = {
	set_variable = { global.influence_one = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_ten = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_hundred = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_thousand = EUM.influence_to_add }

	add_to_variable = { global.influence_one = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_ten = 10 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_hundred = 100 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_thousand = 1000 }

	set_variable = { global.influence_one_subtract = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_ten_subtract = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_hundred_subtract = EUM.influence_to_add }
	set_variable = { global.influence_thousand_subtract = EUM.influence_to_add }

	add_to_variable = { global.influence_one_subtract = -1 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_ten_subtract = -10 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_hundred_subtract = -100 }
	add_to_variable = { global.influence_thousand_subtract = -1000 }
}

	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_right_incorrect
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_left_incorrect
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_syndie_incorrect
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_totalist_incorrect
	}
	
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_right
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_left
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_syndie
	}

		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_totalist
	}
}

AUS_socialist_republic_modifier_tot = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = totalist
		}
		add_power_balance_modifier = {
			id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
			modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_totalist
		}
		else = {
			add_power_balance_modifier = {
				id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
				modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_totalist_incorrect
			}
		}
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {
		id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_right_incorrect
	}
	remove_power_balance_modifier = {

		modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_left_incorrect

AUS_rev_progress_2 = {
	add_to_variable = {
		var = THIS.revolution_progress
		value = 0.02
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = THIS.revolution_progress
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_rev_progress_2_tt
}

AUS_index_subgroup_strengths = {
	add_to_array = {
		array = global.AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
		value = THIS.anarchist_power
	}
	add_to_array = {
		array = global.AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
		value = THIS.unionist_power
	}
	add_to_array = {
		array = global.AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
		value = THIS.DAP_power
	}
	
	
	
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = global.AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
		value = temp_high_power
		index = temp_high_power_index #what?
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
				value = THIS.anarchist_power
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_high_anarchist
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
					value = THIS.unionist_power
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_high_unionist
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_values
						value = THIS.DAP_power
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = AUS_high_DAP
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_fuck_this_ideology_they_unpopular_now_lmaofuckoff = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = totalist
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_totalist_unpopular
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_syndicalist_unpopular
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_radical_socialist_unpopular
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_social_democrat_unpopular
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_social_liberal_unpopular
	}
	
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_market_liberal_unpopular
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_social_conservative_unpopular
	}
	
	
	if = {
		limit = {

	}
	
	if = {

	if = {

	}
}

BOTDE_create_austrian_emperor = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_Kaiser_Otto_I }

	}

AUS_restore_danubian_federation = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = default_danubian_state
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_state_core = PREV
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = default_danubian_state
			NOT = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_state_claim = PREV
		}
	}
}

AUS_coalition_value = {
	add_to_variable = {
		var = AUS.coalition_value
		value = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = AUS.coalition_value
				value = 3
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = HUN
					tag = CRO
					tag = CZE
					tag = GAL
				}
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction = no
				has_opinion = {
					target = AUS
					value < 65
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.169
				days = 5
				random_hours = 96
			}
		}
	}
}

HSR_setup_civil_war = {
	hidden_effect = {
		start_civil_war = {
			### basics ###
			ideology = totalist
			size = 0.33
			army_ratio = 0.4
			navy_ratio = 0.5

			### states ###
			capital = 43
			states = { 1107 1106 155 784 1111 }		

			### characters ###
			keep_all_characters = yes

			### effects ###
			set_temp_variable = { HUN_civil_war_target = THIS }
		}

		#move all socialists to revolter
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = HSR_leader }
			set_nationality = var:HUN_civil_war_target
		}		
		
		#setup revolter
		var:HUN_civil_war_target = {
			#set cosmetic tag
			save_global_event_target_as = HUN_soviet_republic
			set_cosmetic_tag = HSR
			
			set_war_support = 0.7
			
			#set leaders and ideology
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 25
				radical_socialist = 11
				syndicalist = 21
				social_democrat = 6
				social_liberal = 0
				market_liberal = 4
				social_conservative = 9
				authoritarian_democrat = 14
				paternal_autocrat = 0
				national_populist = 10
			}		
			load_focus_tree = { tree = HUN_focus keep_completed = yes }
			
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				HUN_Sandor_Garbai_hog_syn
				HUN_Erik_Molnar_for_tot
				HUN_Erno_Gero_eco_tot
				HUN_Matyas_Rakosi_sec_tot
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Béla Kun"
				desc = "POLITICS_BELA_KUN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/HUN/Portrait_HUN_Bela_Kun.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authcom_subtype
			}
			
			XXA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = HSR_leader }
					set_nationality = var:HUN_civil_war_target
				}
			}
			#spawn units
			#HSR_units = yes
		}
		
		set_political_party = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0 }
	}
}

CONST_generic_peace_post = { #Expansion and some things for post-collapse countries after they are freed
	if = {
		limit = { tag = CPU }
		add_state_claim = 1319
		add_state_claim = 1314
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = BAN }
		add_state_claim = 45
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = HNZ }
		add_state_claim = 1111
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = CRO }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 104
					state = 794
					state = 1099
					state = 1128
					state = 1141
					state = 1142
					state = 1143
					state = 1145
				}
				is_fully_controlled_by = CRO
			}
			transfer_state_to = CRO
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = HUN }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 76
					state = 789
					state = 1112
					state = 1117
					state = 1118
				}
				is_fully_controlled_by = HUN
			}
			transfer_state_to = HUN
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = BOS }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BOS
				is_fully_controlled_by = BOS
			}
			transfer_state_to = BOS
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = SKS }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SKS
				is_fully_controlled_by = SKS
			}
			transfer_state_to = SKS
		}
	}
	if = { #things
		limit = {
			ROOT = { tag = CRO }
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = BOS
					tag = SKS
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { exists = yes } }
			CRO = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = national_populist }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = CRO_republic
				}
				set_country_flag = CRO_won_independence
				set_country_flag = CRO_federation_dead
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { tag = SER }
			FROM = { tag = CRO }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { exists = yes } }
			CRO = {
				set_country_flag = CRO_won_independence
				set_country_flag = CRO_federation_dead
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 103
						state = 163
						state = 1098
						state = 1099
						state = 1105
						state = 1206
					}
					is_owned_by = FROM
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 794
						state = 1128
						state = 1270
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}

AUS_ausgleich_ending_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ausgleich_austria_pays
				has_global_flag = ausgleich_illyria_pays
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = ausgleich_austria_pays }
			AUS = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = AUS_gleich_payments
					days = 120
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = ausgleich_austria_pays
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = ausgleich_illyria_pays }
			CRO = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = AUS_gleich_payments
					days = 120
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = ausgleich_illyria_pays
		}
		HUN = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_gleich_payments_recipient
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_reform_customs_union }
		AUS = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_gleich_reforms_customs_union
				days = 120
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = AUS_reform_customs_union
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = ausgleich_AUS_transfer_german_hungary }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = HUN
				state = 784
			}
			transfer_state_to = AUS
		}
		clr_global_flag = ausgleich_AUS_transfer_german_hungary
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania_minorities }
		AUS_divide_hungary_effect = yes
		AUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.59
				hours = 12
				random_hours = 24
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_illyria_promoted_AUS }
		CRO = {
			set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CRO_special_status
				add_idea = AUS_cisleithanian_sphere
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_illyria_promoted_AUS
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_transleithanian_illyria }
		CRO = {
			get_current_government_type = yes
			end_puppet = CRO
			HUN = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CRO
					autonomy_state = botde_transleithania
				}
			}
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
			set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CRO_special_status
				add_idea = AUS_transleithanian_sphere
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = AUS_transleithanian_illyria
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = ausgleich_eu_illyria }
		CRO = {
			set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CRO_special_status
				add_idea = CRO_proto_european_state
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = ausgleich_eu_illyria
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_small }
		AUS_ausgleich_small_common_army_effect = yes
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_small
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_medium }
		AUS_ausgleich_medium_common_army_effect = yes
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_medium
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_large }
		AUS_ausgleich_large_common_army_effect = yes
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_large
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_small }
		AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_small_effect = yes
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_small
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_medium }
		AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_medium_effect = yes
		clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_medium

	if = {

}
AUS_ausgleich_small_common_army_effect = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = AUS
				has_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hates_army_policy }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = AUS_common_army_law_small_tt
				if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = undisturbed_isolation
						has_idea = isolation
						has_idea = civilian_economy
					}
				}
				add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
			}
			else = {
				add_one_random_military_factory = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = disarmed_nation
						has_idea = volunteer_only
					}
				}
				add_ideas = limited_conscription
			}
			else = {
				add_manpower = 25000
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_ausgleich_const_revolt_success_effect = {
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.ausgleich_attendants
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_num = THIS.subject_revolt_progress }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_num < 0.5 }
			check_variable = { global.ausgleich_attendants^num > 3 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_num < 0.75 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_num > 1.5 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_num > 2 }
			check_variable = { global.ausgleich_attendants^num > 3 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = -1
		}
	}
}
AUS_ausgleich_common_army_law_unity_small_effect = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = AUS_common_army_unity_small_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
				NOT = {
					tag = AUS
					has_country_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hates_army_policy
				}
			}
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = AUS
				stockpile_ratio = 0.2
				army_ratio = 0.2
				navy_ratio = 0.2
				air_ratio = 0.2
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_common_army_reform_payment
				days = 60
			}
		}
	}
	AUS = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = AUS_common_army_reform
			days = 60
		}
	}
}

				army_ratio = 0.35

				idea = AUS_common_army_reform_payment
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}
	AUS = {

			idea = AUS_common_army_reform
			days = 120
		}
	}
}

AUS_restore_BOH_after_revolt_effect = {
	AUS = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CZE
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = PGU
				}
			}
			CZE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = CZE
			autonomy_state = botde_constituent
		}
	}
	CZE = {
		set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_military_gov
		BOTDE_create_austrian_emperor = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			name = CZE_paternal_autocrat_party_military_gov
			long_name = CZE_paternal_autocrat_party_military_gov_long
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = junta_subtype
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_50 = yes
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = BOH_assert_bohemian_self_determination
			uncomplete_children = yes
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		remove_ideas = {
			CZE_czech_revolution
			BOH_legacy_of_coronation_2
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CZE_Alois_Podhajsky_hog_pau
			AUS_part_of_the_Empire
			AUS_cisleithanian_sphere
			BOH_legacy_of_coronation
		}
		clr_country_flag = CZE_will_revolt
		clr_country_flag = CONST_no_evidenzbureau
		set_country_flag = CONST_proper
		set_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
		set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_CZE_revolt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = CZE } }
			}
			add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = CZE }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
			}
			AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
		}
		set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 4 }
		set_variable = { CZE.subject_revolt_progress = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { CZE.extra_value = -0.015 }
	}
}
AUS_restore_HUN_after_ausgleich_revolt_effect = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = AUS_restore_HUN_after_ausgleich_revolt_effect_tt
		AUS = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HUN
					if = {
						limit = {
							AUS = { has_country_flag = HUN_ausgleich_revolt_deal_with_minorities }
						}
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = SVK
							is_core_of = TRS
							is_core_of = CPU
							state = 784
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = HUN
				autonomy_state = botde_transleithania
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hungarian_revolt }
				set_global_flag = HUN_revolted_during_ausgleich
				clr_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hungarian_revolt
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hates_army_policy }
				clr_country_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hates_army_policy
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hungarian_revolt
					has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_ongoing
				}
				set_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
				set_country_flag = HUN_always_accept_ausgleich_demands
				clr_country_flag = CONST_no_evidenzbureau
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_boycotted_ausgleich }
					clr_global_flag = HUN_boycotted_ausgleich
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { global.ausgleich_attendants = THIS.id } } }
					add_to_array = {
						array = global.ausgleich_attendants
						value = THIS.id
						index = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = HUN } } }
					add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = HUN }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { AUS = { AUS_DWV_member = yes } }
				AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { AUS = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research } }
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				name = HUN_paternal_autocrat_party_military_gov
				long_name = HUN_paternal_autocrat_party_military_gov_long
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = junta_subtype
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				HUN_Joseph_August_von_Habsburg_hog_pau
				HUN_Endre_Bajcsy_Zsilinszky_for_pau
				HUN_Imre_Oltvanyi_eco_ade
				HUN_Kalman_Daranyi_de_Pusztaszentgyoergyi_sec_pau
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_military_gov
			BOTDE_create_austrian_emperor = yes
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_30 = yes
			set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 2 }
			set_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress = 0.45 }
			set_variable = { Karl_Portrait_Var = 6 }
			add_ideas = {
				AUS_part_of_the_Empire
				AUS_HUN_military_government_idea
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				HUN_reactionary_rebels_idea
			}
			set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_HUN_revolt
			set_country_flag = CONST_proper
			set_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FIU = { has_country_flag = FIU_return_puppet_to_hungary_after_revolt } }
			FIU = { get_current_government_type = yes }
			end_puppet = FIU
			HUN = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FIU
					autonomy_state = botde_fiume
				}
				add_ideas = HUN_fiume_economy
			}
			FIU = {
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				clr_country_flag = FIU_return_puppet_to_hungary_after_revolt
			}
		}
	}
}
AUS_restore_CRO_after_revolt_effect = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = CRO
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = AUS
				is_owned_by = HUN
			}
		}
		transfer_state_to = CRO
	}
	AUS = {
		set_autonomy = {
			target = CRO
			autonomy_state = botde_occupied
		}
	}
	CRO = {
		set_cosmetic_tag = CRO_occupied
		BOTDE_create_austrian_emperor = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			name = CRO_occupied_paternal_autocrat_party
			long_name = CRO_occupied_paternal_autocrat_party_long
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = junta_subtype
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			CRO_Stjepan_Sarkotic_hog_pau
			CRO_Mladen_Lorkovic_for_pau
			CRO_Jozo_Dumandzic_eco_pau
			CRO_Edo_Bulat_sec_pau
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		remove_ideas = {
			CRO_for_illyria
			CRO_guerilla_war
		}
		add_ideas = {
			AUS_part_of_the_Empire
			AUS_cisleithanian_sphere
		}
		complete_national_focus = CRO_complete_loyalty_to_vienna
		clr_country_flag = CRO_will_revolt
		clr_country_flag = CONST_no_evidenzbureau
		set_country_flag = CONST_proper
		set_country_flag = no_minority_revolt
		set_country_flag = CRO_is_occupied
		set_global_flag = AUS_no_more_CRO_revolt
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { global.constituents_array = CRO } } }
			add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = CRO }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AUS = { AUS_DWV_member = yes } }
			AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CRO_democracy }
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = CRO_democracy
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 4 }
		set_variable = { CRO.subject_revolt_progress = 0.1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_has_revolted_before }
			set_variable = { CRO.extra_value = -0.015 }
		}
	}
}

AUS_unoccupy_ROM_effect = {
	AUS = {
		set_autonomy = {
			target = ROM
			autonomous_state = botde_satellite
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausfor.214
			days = 1
			random_hours = 24
		}
	}
	ROM = {
		set_cosmetic_tag = ROM_AUS_kingdom
		set_country_flag = ROM_restored_kingdom_under_AUS
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = ROM_social_democrat_party_PNT
			long_name = ROM_social_democrat_party_PNT_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			name = ROM_social_liberal_party_PNT
			long_name = ROM_social_liberal_party_PNT_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			name = ROM_social_conservative_party_PNT
			long_name = ROM_social_conservative_party_PNT_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			name = ROM_AUS_kingdom_paternal_autocrat_party
			long_name = ROM_AUS_kingdom_paternal_autocrat_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			name = ROM_AUS_kingdom_national_populist_party
			long_name = ROM_AUS_kingdom_national_populist_party_long
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ROM_PNT_madgearu
			ROM_first_elect_PNT = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anton von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAR/Portrait_CAR_Archduke_Anton_of_Austria.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = socdem_agrarianism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = {
					OR = {
						has_government = social_liberal
						has_government = market_liberal
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ROM_PNT_maniu
			ROM_first_elect_PNT = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anton von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAR/Portrait_CAR_Archduke_Anton_of_Austria.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = soclib_agrarianism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = {
					OR = {
						has_government = social_conservative
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ROM_PNT_vaida
			ROM_first_elect_PNT = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anton von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAR/Portrait_CAR_Archduke_Anton_of_Austria.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = soccon_agrarianism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = {
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anton von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAR/Portrait_CAR_Archduke_Anton_of_Austria.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_junta_subtype
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anton von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAR/Portrait_CAR_Archduke_Anton_of_Austria.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_junta_subtype
			}
		}
		set_popularities = {
			totalist = 3
			syndicalist = 8
			radical_socialist = 5
			social_democrat = 21
			social_liberal = 8
			market_liberal = 5
			social_conservative = 17
			authoritarian_democrat = 16
			paternal_autocrat = 12
			national_populist = 5
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		remove_ideas = {
			ROM_austrian_occupation
		}
	}
}

AUS_5bw_AUS_victory_SER_peacedeal = {
	AUS_remove_all_SER_state_revolt_target_modifiers = yes
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_claimed_by = SER
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CRO
				is_owned_by = ALB
				is_owned_by = MNT
				is_owned_by = HUN
				is_owned_by = AUS
				is_owned_by = SKS
				is_owned_by = BOS
			}
		}
		remove_claim_by = SER
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = SER
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CRO
				is_owned_by = ALB
				is_owned_by = MNT
				is_owned_by = HUN
				is_owned_by = AUS
				is_owned_by = SKS
				is_owned_by = BOS
			}
		}
		remove_core_of = SER
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = MNT
				MNT = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				state = 1269
			}
			transfer_state_to = MNT
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GRE
				GRE = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				state = 763
			}
			transfer_state_to = GRE
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = ALB
				ALB = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 765
					state = 1271
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = ALB
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = BUL
				BUL = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 106
					state = 743
					state = 763
					state = 767
					state = 841
					state = 1271
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = BUL
		}
	}
	if = {

		if = {
			limit = { MCD = { exists = no } }
			set_global_flag = MCD_didnt_exist_before_5BW_peace
		}
		every_state = {

					state = 106
					state = 731
					state = 1271
				}
			}
			add_core_of = MCD
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { state = 841 }
			add_claim_by = MCD
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = MCD
					is_claimed_by = MCD
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = MCD
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_state = { is_owned_by = MCD }
			has_global_flag = MCD_didnt_exist_before_5BW_peace
		}
		AUS_occupy_MCD_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			MNT = { exists = no }
			OR = {
				has_war_with = CRO
				CRO = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 105
					state = 1097
					state = 1269
					state = 1270
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = CRO
		}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				state = 107
				state = 108
			}
		}
		transfer_state_to = AUS
	}
}

AUS_5bw_SER_victory_SER_peacedeal = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = AUS }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = SER
					is_core_of = SER
				}
				NOT = { is_core_of = SLO }
				is_owned_by = AUS
			}
			transfer_state_to = SER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = HUN }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = SER
					is_core_of = SER
					state = 45
					state = 875
				}
				is_owned_by = HUN
			}
			transfer_state_to = SER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = CRO }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				CRO = {
					all_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = SER
							is_core_of = SER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CRO = {
				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = AUS }
				every_scientist = { set_nationality = AUS }
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = AUS
					size = 0.5
					army_ratio = 0.5
					navy_ratio = 0.5
					air_ratio = 0.5
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = HUN
					size = 0.5
					army_ratio = 0.5
					navy_ratio = 0.5
					air_ratio = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.168
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = SER
					is_core_of = SER
				}
				is_owned_by = CRO
			}
			transfer_state_to = SER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = MNT }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = SER
					is_core_of = SER
				}
				is_owned_by = MNT
			}
			transfer_state_to = SER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = FIU
				AND = {
					has_war_with = var:FIU.overlord
					var:FIU.overlord = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FIU = {
					all_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = SER
							is_core_of = SER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FIU = {
				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = AUS }
				every_scientist = { set_nationality = AUS }
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = AUS
					size = 1
					army_ratio = 1
					navy_ratio = 1
					air_ratio = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = SER
					is_core_of = SER
				}
				is_owned_by = FIU
			}
			transfer_state_to = SER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_with = ALB }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GRE }
			every_state = {
				limit = { state = 766 }
				transfer_state_to = GRE
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = ALB }
				transfer_state_to = SER
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = SER
						is_core_of = SER
					}
					is_owned_by = ALB
				}
				transfer_state_to = SER
			}
		}
	}
	AUS_remove_all_SER_state_revolt_target_modifiers = yes
}
