AUS_remove_all_SER_state_revolt_target_modifiers = {
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_srpska_resistance } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_srpska_resistance }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_bosnia_resistance } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_bosnia_resistance }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_target_lands_resistance } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_target_lands_resistance }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = SER_resistance_crap_done
			is_core_of = owner
			has_active_resistance = yes
		}
		cancel_resistance = yes
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = SER_resistance_crap_done
			has_variable = THIS.success_value_opp
		}
		clear_variable = THIS.success_value_opp
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			is_in_array = { global.bp_occupied_tag_array_SER = THIS }
			has_variable = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0 }
	}
}
AUS_remove_all_ROM_state_revolt_target_modifiers = {
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_target_lands_resistance } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_target_lands_resistance }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_transylvanian_resistance } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_transylvanian_resistance }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_transylvanian_collaboration } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ROM_transylvanian_collaboration }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = TRS
				is_core_of = BUK
				is_core_of = BAN
			}
			is_core_of = owner
			has_active_resistance = yes
		}
		cancel_resistance = yes
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = TRS
				is_core_of = BUK
				is_core_of = BAN
			}
			has_variable = THIS.success_value_opp
		}
		clear_variable = THIS.success_value_opp
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = TRS
				tag = BAN
				tag = BUK
			}
			has_variable = THIS.subject_revolt_progress
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0 }
	}
}

AUS_meta_BM_reduce = {
	set_temp_variable = { AUS_BM_value_temp = AUS_BM_value }
	add_to_variable = { AUS.AUS_BM_value = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { AUS.AUS_BM_value > 5 } }
		remove_ideas = AUS_bm_5
	}
	else = {
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = AUS_bm_reduce
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					swap_ideas = {
						add_idea = AUS_bm_[AUS_BM_value]
						remove_idea = AUS_bm_[AUS_BM_value_temp]
					}
				}
				AUS_BM_value = "[?AUS_BM_value]"
				AUS_BM_value_temp = "[?AUS_BM_value_temp]"
			}
		}
	}
}

AUS_blutpakt_coalition_effect = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = blutpakt_coalition_value_raise
	add_to_variable = { global.blutpakt_coalition_value = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { global.blutpakt_coalition_value = 2 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_blutpakt_condemnations }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = BOTDE_blutpakt_condemnations
			every_collection_element = {
				input = collection:botde_constituents_and_minorites_countries
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = AUS
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
					}
					exists = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.187 #Blutpakt Worries
					days = 3
					random_days = 11
				}
			}
			SER = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.187 #Blutpakt Worries
					days = 3
					random_days = 11
				}
			}
			ROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.187 #Blutpakt Worries
					days = 3
					random_days = 11
				}
			}
			every_allied_country = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.188
					days = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { global.blutpakt_coalition_value = 3 }
			has_global_flag = BOTDE_blutpakt_condemnations
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SER = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			SER = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.189
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CZE = {
						OR = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							AND = {
								is_subject = no
								is_in_faction = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.189
						days = 2
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_subject = no
							is_in_faction = no
							has_country_flag = BOTDE_blutpakt_condemnation
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
SER_shoot_down_a_airplane_effect = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = SER_seek_chetnik_ties_tt
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.SER_target_states
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_state_flag = SER_resistance_crap_done } }
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = SKS }
					force_enable_resistance = { occupier = var:THIS.owner occupied = SKS }
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_resistance = no }
						start_resistance = SKS
						set_compliance = 10
						set_resistance = 10
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = BOS
						NOT = { is_core_of = SKS }
					}
					force_enable_resistance = { occupier = var:THIS.owner occupied = BOS }
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_resistance = no }
						start_resistance = BOS
						set_compliance = 10
						set_resistance = 10
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = SLO }
					force_enable_resistance = { occupier = var:THIS.owner occupied = SLO }
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_resistance = no }
						start_resistance = SLO
						set_compliance = 10
						set_resistance = 10
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SER_target_lands_resistance }
				set_variable = { SER_target_lands_resistance_target = 0 }
				set_variable = { SER_target_lands_resistance_activity = 0 }
				set_variable = { SER_target_lands_resistance_garrison = 0 }
				#owner = {
				#	if = {
				#		limit = {
				#			NOT = { has_country_flag = SER_receives_oopsiedaisy }
				#		}
				#		country_event = bdeausint.whateverman
				#		set_country_flag = { flag = SER_receives_oopsiedaisy days = 2 value = 1 }
				#	}
				#}
			}
			set_state_flag = SER_resistance_crap_done
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = CRO
				}
				AUS_is_constituent = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.90
				days = 1
				random_hours = 144
			}
		}
	}
}
SER_revolt_mission_timeout_effect = {
	event_target:BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag = {
		set_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt
		capital_scope = {
			owner = {
				set_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
				save_event_target_as = BOTDE_RVO_temp
			}
		}
		do_minority_revolt_setup = yes
		clr_country_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_start
		get_current_government_type = yes
		ROOT = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = kr_integrated_puppet
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = event_target:BOTDE_RVO_temp
				type = annex_everything
			}
			PREV = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = event_target:BOTDE_RVO_temp
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_idea = BOTDE_delenda_est } }
				hidden_effect = { add_timed_idea = { idea = BOTDE_delenda_est days = 240 } }
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		SKS_revolt_units_SER = yes
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = { check_variable = { THIS.extra_divs > 0 } }
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Chetnik Detachment" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Chetnik Detachment"
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
						support = {
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = { 
							division = "name = \"Četnički Odred\" division_template = \"Chetnik Detachment\" start_experience_factor = 0.65" 
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { THIS.extra_divs = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = BOTDE_delenda_est } }
			hidden_effect = { add_timed_idea = { idea = BOTDE_delenda_est days = 240 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = BOS }
			set_cosmetic_tag = BOS_SER_revolt
			if = {
				limit = { SER = { has_government = national_populist } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = national_populist }
				increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SER = { has_government = paternal_autocrat } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
				increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
			}
			else = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SKS }
			if = {
				limit = { SER = { has_government = national_populist } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = national_populist }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SLO }
			set_cosmetic_tag = SLO_revolt
			if = {
				limit = { SER = { has_government = national_populist } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = national_populist }
			}
			else = { set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat } }
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_50 = yes
		}
	}
	clear_global_event_target = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
	clr_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = SER
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				fifth_balkan_war = no
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.101
				hours = 2
				random_hours = 3
			}
		}
		if = { #If Romania is an AI, figure out its balance of power and start some revolts to help out Serbian player or if Romania never joined the BP
			limit = {				
				SER = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_ai = no 
							is_in_faction_with = ROM
						}
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROM }
					}
				}
				ROM = { is_ai = yes }
			}
			ROM_help_serb_player_revolt = yes
		}
	}
}

AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_prelude_setup = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 39
				state = 152
				state = 153
				state = 783
				state = 836
				state = 942
			}
		}
		transfer_state_to = AWR
	}
	AWR = {
		activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_headsup
		set_cosmetic_tag = AWR_vril
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jörg Lanz von Liebenfels"
			desc = "POLITICS_LIEBENFELS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Liebenfels.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = ariosophy_subtype
		}
		set_popularities = {
			totalist = 8
			syndicalist = 12
			radical_socialist = 3
			authoritarian_democrat = 5
			paternal_autocrat = 12
			national_populist = 60
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			AWR_kaisertreuen
			AWR_leftist_disunity
			AUS_postcollapse_army_idea
			AUS_militias
		}
		add_ideas = {
			AUS_purity_2
			AUS_theozoology
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { num_divisions = AWR.extra_units_at_civil_war_start }
				add_to_temp_variable = { num_divisions = AUS.ordo_novi_templi_presence }
				check_variable = { num_divisions > 0 }
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Ordo Novi Templi Paramilitärische Division\" division_template = \"Infanteriedivision\" start_manpower_factor = 0.75"
					owner = AWR
					count = num_divisions
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no
					id = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}
	AUS = {
		activate_mission = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_headsup
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = AWR
			stockpile_ratio = 0.33
			army_ratio = 0.33
			navy_ratio = 0
			air_ratio = 0.33
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
		}
		every_core_state = { add_core_of = AWR }
	}
}

AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_liebenfels_victory_on_action_effect = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_subject_of = HUN
			}
			is_in_faction_with = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = MNT
			}
			AUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MNT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			MNT = {
				white_peace = AWR
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = AUS
				is_subject_of = HUN
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_autonomy_state = botde_constituent }
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_constituent_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_autonomy_state = botde_satellite }
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_satellite_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = botde_transleithania
				NOT = { tag = HUN }
			}
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_transleithania_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = HUN }
			set_country_flag = BOTDE_was_subject_of_HUN_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_transleithania_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
				clr_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_transleithania_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_subject_of_HUN_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 } }
			end_puppet = PREV
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_constituent_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		get_current_government_type = yes
		HUN = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_constituent
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_satellite_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		get_current_government_type = yes
		HUN = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_satellite
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_transleithania_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		get_current_government_type = yes
		HUN = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_transleithania
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
	}
	HUN = {
		set_faction_leader = yes
		add_ideas = {
			AUS_habsburgs_last_stand
			AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_idea
		}
		set_major = yes
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_ai = no } }
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	FROM = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = AUS
					is_core_of = HUN
					is_core_of = CZE
					is_core_of = CRO
					is_core_of = GAL
				}
			}
			add_state_core = PREV
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		create_faction_from_template = {
			template = faction_template_austria
			name = faction_aus_vril
			icon = GFX_faction_vril
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_international_isolation
		annex_country = {
			target = ROOT
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		set_capital = {
			state = 1137
			remember_old_capital = no
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = HUN
				is_subject_of = HUN
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}
AUS_liebenfels_civil_war_liebenfels_loss_after_capping_AUS_effect = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_owned_by = ROOT
			is_core_of = AUS
		}
		transfer_state_to = AUS
	}
	ROOT = {
		dismantle_faction = yes
	}
	FROM = {
		set_major = no
		add_to_faction = AUS
		remove_ideas = {
			AUS_habsburgs_last_stand
		}
	}
	AUS = {
		set_major = yes
		set_faction_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ai = no } }
			change_tag_from = FROM
		}
		AUS_PNEO_coup_effect = yes
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of = HUN
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_subject_of_HUN_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		}
		end_puppet = PREV
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_constituent_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		get_current_government_type = yes
		AUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_constituent
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_constituent_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_satellite_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		get_current_government_type = yes
		AUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV

			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes

				tag = HUN
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BOTDE_was_subject_of_HUN_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2 }
		}
		get_current_government_type = yes
		AUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomous_state = botde_transleithania
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		clr_country_flag = BOTDE_was_botde_transleithania_before_liebenfels_civil_war_part_2
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { is_core_of = ROOT }
		ROOT = { remove_state_core = PREV }
	}
	clr_global_flag = AUS_liebenfels_civil_war
}

AUS_start_civil_war_effect = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = AUS_civil_war_start_tt
		every_owned_state = {
			add_core_of = AWR
		}
		AWR = {
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			transfer_state = 4
			transfer_state = 152
			declare_war_on = {
				target = AUS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_collapse_DM_stays
			}
			HUN = {
				country_event = bdeausint.59
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			AWR = {
				complete_national_focus = AUS_the_danube_runs_red
				AWR_units = yes
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.72
					days = 30
					random_hours = 1000
				}
			}
			transfer_units_fraction= {
				target = AWR
				size = 0.2
				stockpile_ratio = 0.8
				army_ratio = 0.2
				navy_ratio = 0
				air_ratio = 0.3
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			}
			news_event = bdeausnews.8
			#country_event = {
			#	id = bdeausint.126
			#	days = 2
			#}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_DOLLFUSS
					has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.93
					days = 3
					random_hours = 48
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = national_populist
						has_government = paternal_autocrat
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_government = social_conservative
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.155
					days = 20
					random_hours = 100
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = AUS_civil_war
			add_ideas = AUS_civil_war_idea_AUS
			AWR = { add_ideas = AUS_civil_war_idea_AWR }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AUS_SDAPO_embraced_revolution
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
				AWR = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						popularity = 0.1
					}
					set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democrat }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
				AWR = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialis
						popularity = 0.1
					}
					set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialist }
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = AUS_pataut_habsburg
				long_name = AUS_pataut_habsburg_long
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Karl I"
				desc = "POLITICS_KARL_BOTDE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Karl_I.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				AUS_karl_von_habsburg_hog_pau
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AWR = {
						OR = {
							has_government = radical_socialist
							has_government = social_democrat
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { party_popularity@totalist > party_popularity@syndicalist }
					check_variable = { party_popularity@totalist = party_popularity@syndicalist }
				}
			}
			AWR = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.1 }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = totalist
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			AWR = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.1 }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = syndicalist
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AUS_SDAPO_embraced_revolution
			}
			AWR = {
				set_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
				#country_event = {
				#	id = bdeausint.68
				#	days = 7
				#	random = 80
				#}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = AWR
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.95
				days = 7
				random_hours = 48
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.73 #Civil war taking too long
				days = 240
			}
		}
	}
}

		remove_from_array = { global.minorities_array = ENG }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { AUS.austria_minority_array = ENG } }
		remove_from_array = { AUS.austria_minority_array = ENG }
	}

		add_to_array = {
			array = global.constituents_array

			index = 2
		}
	}

		add_to_array = { global.AUS_all_possible_array = ENG }
	}
	country_event = constituents.51

	}
}
AUS_display_weekly_collpase_modifiers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier < 10 } }
		if = { #base value
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_over }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 0.002 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = AUS_root_out_class_hatred
						has_completed_focus = AUS_to_these_united_states
						has_completed_focus = AUS_test_of_time
						has_completed_focus = AUS_charity_and_unity
					}
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 0.002 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_base_value
		}
		if = { #ruling party pop
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 1 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = party_popularity@ruling_party }
			multiply_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.01 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_party_pop
			}
		}
		if = { # stability
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 2 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = stability }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.03 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_stability
			}
		}
		if = { #war exhaust
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 3 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = global.extra_value_war_exhaust }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_war_exhaust
			}
		}
		if = { #federalizing
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 4 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = global.extra_collapse_federalizing }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_federalizing
			}
		}
		if = { #revolt rate modifier
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 5 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = modifier@BOTDE_revolt_rate_modifier }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = extra_value }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_revolt_rate_modifier
			}
		}
		if = { #fifth balkan war
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 6 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { fifth_balkan_war = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.005 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_fifth_balkan_war
			}
		}
		if = { #continuous focus
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 7 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_AUS_continuous_collapse_decrease_flag }
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_continuous_focus
			}
		}
		if = { #result (uses actual calculation)
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 8 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change = 1 }
			THIS = { AUS_do_revolt_rate_rise = yes }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = revolt_progress_change }
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_total
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { current_modifier = 1 }
		AUS_display_weekly_collpase_modifiers_effect = yes
	}
}
AUS_display_weekly_const_revolt_modifiers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier < 13 } }
		if = { #base value
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_over }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_base_value
		}
		if = { # stability
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 1 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = num_of_factories }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_var = num_battalions }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_var_2 = AUS.stability }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_var_3 = stability }
			add_to_temp_variable = { temp_var_2 = -1.2 }
			divide_temp_variable = { temp_var_3 = 3 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { temp_var_2 = temp_var_3 }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 120 }
			divide_temp_variable = { temp_var = 10000 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp_var_2 = -3.5 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = temp_var }
			multiply_temp_variable = { modifier = temp_var_2 }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_stability
			}
		}
		if = { #paramilitaries
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 2 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = num_battalions }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 10000 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_battalions
			}
		}
		if = { #austrian paramilitaries
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 3 } }

			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = -50000 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }

			}
		}
		if = { #austrian factories
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 4 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = AUS.num_of_factories }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = -7500 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_aus_factories
			}
		}
		if = { #evidenzbureau

			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }

				limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_evidenzbureau
			}
		}
		if = { #war exhaustion
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 6 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = global.extra_value_war_exhaust }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_war_exhaust
			}
		}
		if = { #federalizing
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 7 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = global.extra_collapse_federalizing }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_federalizing
			}
		}
		if = { #revolt rate modifier
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 8 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = modifier@BOTDE_revolt_rate_modifier }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = extra_value }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_revolt_rate_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 9 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_operative_leader = { operative_leader_mission = counter_intelligence }
					NOT = {
						is_preparing_operation = { target = any_country }
						is_running_operation  = { target = any_country }
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.03 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_counter_intel
			}
		}
		if = { #fifth balkan war
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 10 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { fifth_balkan_war = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.005 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_fifth_balkan_war
			}
		}
		if = { #continuous focus
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 11 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_AUS_continuous_collapse_decrease_flag }
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_continuous_focus
			}
		}
		if = { #result (uses actual calculation)
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 12 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change = 1 }
			CONST_do_additional_revolt_progress = yes
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = CONST_revolt_rate_rising }
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_total
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { current_modifier = 1 }
		AUS_display_weekly_const_revolt_modifiers_effect = yes
	}
}
AUS_display_weekly_minority_revolt_modifiers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier < 10 } }
		if = { #base value
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_base_value
		}
		if = { #collapse progress
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 1 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = AUS.subject_revolt_progress }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 90 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_aus_collapse_value
			}
		}
		if = { #resistance
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 2 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = avg_resistance }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 1600 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_state_resistance
			}
		}
		if = { #paramilitaries
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 3 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = paramilitary_value }
			divide_temp_variable = { modifier = 270 } #90 * 3
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_paramilitaries
			}
		}
		if = { #evidenzbureau
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 4 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = no
					capital_scope.owner = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 0.005 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = AUS_evidenzbureau_focus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { modifier = 0.025 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_evidenzbureau
			}
		}
		if = { #continuous focus
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 5 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = BOTDE_AUS_continuous_collapse_decrease_flag }
				add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { modifier = 0 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_continuous_focus
			}
		}
		if = { #result (uses actual calculation)
			limit = { check_variable = { current_modifier = 6 } }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { do_not_apply_revolt_change = 1 }
			CONST_do_additional_revolt_progress = yes
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier = CONST_revolt_rate_rising }
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifier_total
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { current_modifier = 1 }
		AUS_display_weekly_minority_revolt_modifiers_effect = yes
	}
}
AUS_display_weekly_collpase_modifiers_effect_tooltip = { #uses a effect tooltip to display the below because hoi4 jank
	custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_const_tooltip_modifiers
	set_temp_variable = { current_modifier = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { THIS = { tag = AUS } }
		effect_tooltip = { AUS_display_weekly_collpase_modifiers_effect = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			THIS = {
				NOT = { tag = AUS }
				AUS_is_constituent = yes
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { AUS_display_weekly_const_revolt_modifiers_effect = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			THIS = {
				NOT = { tag = AUS }
				AUS_is_minority = yes
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { AUS_display_weekly_minority_revolt_modifiers_effect = yes }
	}
}

		VNC = { set_country_flag = AUS_federalize_flag }
	}

		LOM = { set_country_flag = AUS_federalize_flag }
	}

AUS_austro_american_alliance_form_effect = {
	every_faction_member = { add_to_temp_array = { temp_faction_members = THIS.id } }
	if = {
		limit = { has_faction_research_unlocked = yes }
		set_country_flag = temp_add_faction_research
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_faction_military_unlocked = yes }
		set_country_flag = temp_add_faction_military
	}
	dismantle_faction = yes
	set_global_flag = AUS_austro_american_alliance_flag
	meta_effect = {
		debug = yes
		text = {
			create_faction_from_template = {
				template = faction_template_austro_american_alliance
				name = [FACTION_NAME]
				icon = [FACTION_ICON]
			}
		}
		FACTION_NAME = "[AUS_get_US_ally_faction_name]"
		FACTION_ICON = "[AUS_get_US_ally_faction_icon]"
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { temp_faction_members = THIS.id } }
		AUS = {
			add_to_faction = PREV
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = faction_traitor
			}
		}
	}
	add_to_faction = FROM
	add_faction_influence_ratio = 0.33
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = temp_add_faction_research }
		set_faction_research_unlocked = yes
		clr_country_flag = temp_add_faction_research
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = temp_add_faction_military }
		set_faction_military_unlocked = yes
		clr_country_flag = temp_add_faction_military
	}
}

AUS_create_silesia_effect = {
	SLS = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 66
					state = 67
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = SLS
			add_core_of = SLS
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = SLS_HABSBURG
		set_country_flag = CONST_proper
		add_to_array = { global.constituents_array = THIS }
		set_variable = { THIS.AUS_subject_status = 5 }
		set_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0 }
		set_variable = { THIS.CONST_revolt_rate_rising = -0.015 }
		AUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PREV
				autonomy_state = botde_satellite
			}
		}
		transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_country_flag = rad_socs_arent_syndie } }
				set_country_flag = rad_socs_arent_syndie
			}
			if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = radical_socialist } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialist }
				add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = social_democrat } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democrat }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = social_liberal } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = market_liberal } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = social_conservative } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { overlord = { has_government = paternal_autocrat } }
				set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 2
				syndicalist = 8
				radical_socialist = 10
				social_democrat = 13
				social_liberal = 2
				market_liberal = 8
				social_conservative = 17
				authoritarian_democrat = 20
				paternal_autocrat = 12
				national_populist = 8
			}
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = radsoc_paternal_socialism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = austromarxism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = soclib_agrarianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = marlib_agrarianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_socialism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Albrecht I"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBRECHT_VON_HABSBURG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/Portrait_AUS_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = austropopulism_subtype

		}

			}
		}

		set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_danubia
	}
}

						state = 42
						state = 50
						state = 52
						state = 53
						state = 54
						state = 55
						state = 780
						state = 781
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = AUS
			}
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = AUS
							tag = RUS
							is_ally_with = AUS
							is_ally_with = RUS
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = RUS
			}
		}
	}
}
AUS_upgrade_amount_of_guys_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = temp_num } }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_num = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_num > 1 } }
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = AUS_upgrade_number_of_guys_tt
			for_loop_effect = {
				end = temp_num
				random_unit_leader = {
					add_max_trait = 1
					add_skill_level = 1
					add_logistics = 1
					add_planning = 1
					add_defense = 1
					add_attack = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		random_unit_leader = {
			add_max_trait = 1
			add_skill_level = 1
			add_logistics = 1
			add_planning = 1
			add_defense = 1
			add_attack = 1
		}
	}
}
AUS_decrease_party_pop_if_its_too_popular_effect = {
	set_temp_variable_to_random = temp_decrease
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = temp_decrease
		min = 0.1
		max = 0.2
	}
	set_temp_variable = { coalition_partners_plus_one = coalition_partners^num }
	add_to_temp_variable = { coalition_partners_plus_one = 1 }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp_decrease = coalition_partners_plus_one }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp_decrease = -1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_totalist = yes
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = totalist
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_syndicalist = yes
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = syndicalist
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_radical_socialist = yes
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = radical_socialist
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_social_democrat = yes
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = social_democrat
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = social_liberal
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_market_liberal = yes
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = market_liberal
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = social_conservative
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_authoritarian_democrat = yes
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = authoritarian_democrat
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_paternal_autocrat = yes
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = paternal_autocrat
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_coalition_with_national_populist = yes
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = national_populist
		    popularity = temp_decrease
		}
	}
}

ALA_LIC_buy_alaska_effect = {
	set_country_flag = ALA_purchase_liechtenstein
	create_country_leader = {
		name = "Franz Joseph II"
		desc = "LIC_FRANZ_II_DESC"
		picture = "gfx/leaders/ALA/Portrait_ALA_Franz_Joseph_II.png"
		expire = "1.1.1"
		ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
	}
	set_cosmetic_tag = ALA_LIC
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = paternal_autocrat
		name = ALA_LIC_party
		long_name = ALA_LIC_party_long
	}
	if = {
		limit = { LIC = { is_in_faction = yes } }
		var:LIC.faction_leader = { add_to_faction = ALA }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_power_balance = { id = ALA_two_influences_balance } }
		remove_power_balance = { id = ALA_two_influences_balance }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_ai = yes }
		add_ideas = ALA_clueless_austrians
	}
	get_current_government_type = yes
	LIC = {
		set_autonomy = {
			target = ALA
			autonomy_state = kr_default_puppet
		}
	}
	restore_previous_government_type = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		news_event = {
			id = licnews.5
			days = 1
		}
	}
}
AUS_add_popularity_of_all_parties_in_coalition = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = totalist
				is_in_coalition_with_totalist = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_pop = party_popularity@totalist }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				is_in_coalition_with_syndicalist = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_pop = party_popularity@syndicalist }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
				is_in_coalition_with_radical_socialist = yes
			}

	}
	if = {

				is_in_coalition_with_social_democrat = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_pop = party_popularity@social_democrat }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				is_in_coalition_with_market_liberal = yes

BOTDE_CONST_strike_effect = {
	ROOT_add_five_collapse = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { ROOT.subject_revolt_progress > 0.9 } }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_days = 240 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_times = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { ROOT.subject_revolt_progress > 0.8 } }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_days = 180 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_times = 4 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { ROOT.subject_revolt_progress > 0.7 } }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_days = 120 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_times = 4 }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { temp_days = 90 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_times = 4 }
	}
	add_timed_idea = {
		idea = BOTDE_strike
		days = temp_days
	}
	effect_tooltip = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_effect_happens_a_number_of_times
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
				NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_strike } }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = AUS_strike
				days = temp_days
			}
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = temp_times
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						industrial_complex > 0
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_strike } }
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 0
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_strike } }
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = AUS_strike
						days = temp_days
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
AUS_buy_crete_effect = {
	182 = { transfer_state_to = CRE }
	CRE = { get_current_government_type = yes }
	AUS = {
		set_autonomy = {
			target = CRE
			autonomy_state = botde_occupied
		}
	}
	CRE = {
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = CRE_AUS
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ernst Klepp"
			desc = ""
			picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Ernst_Klepp.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			name = CRE_AUS_paternal_autocrat_party
			long_name = CRE_AUS_paternal_autocrat_party_long
		}
	}
}
